Now, Wang Ying has recruited a total of eight thousand bandit troops. The certain party plans to assign most of them to Li Shouxin's command. Central Government's Two Commemoration Weeks: Xiang Hanping Reports on Guangdong Province; Chairman Lin Gives a Lecture on Studying Science

(Nanjing) The Central Government held its 47th Commemoration Week at 9:00 am on the morning of the 26th. Central Committee members Ye Chucang, Zhang Ji, Feng Yuxiang, Zhou Qigang, He Yingqin, Ma Chaojun, Ju Zheng, Chen Gongbo, Gan Naiguang, Zhu Jiahua, Fang Zhi, Xiang Hanping, Fang Juehui, Wang Boqun, and others, as well as about 700 colleagues working in the ministries, attended. After Chairman Ju Zheng led the ceremony, Xiang Hanping reported in detail on the recent situation in Guangdong Province. The ceremony ended at about 10:00 am. (26th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The National Government held a Commemoration Week on the morning of the 26th. Zhang Ji, Zhou Zhenlin, Deng Jiayan, Wang Boqun, Chen Shuren, Chen Xunyong, Zhang Yipeng, Lü Chao, Wei Huai, and other officials from the National Government and various ministries and departments, totaling about 400 people, attended. After Chairman Lin [Sen] led the ceremony, he gave an impromptu report on "Scientific Research as the Foundation for National Construction." He first explained in detail the passage in the Premier's will: "To restore the status of our nation, in addition to restoring our inherent morality and intelligence, we must learn foreign science in order to stand shoulder to shoulder with Europe and the United States." Next, he stated the functions of science for mankind, including the following: (1) Science is a tool to promote social progress; (2) Science can improve the enjoyment of people's lives; (3) Science is the foundation of material construction; (4) Science is the driving force for national defense. He then stated that the development of science is inevitable, and said that in the past our country's science was not weaker than foreign countries. There are many reasons why we are now behind, but the biggest reason is that our people do not know the importance of science and do not pay attention to scientific research. He said that our country has now been unified, and there will be many construction projects in the future, all of which will require scientific assistance. He hopes that everyone will be enthusiastic about initiating scientific research, so that all construction projects in our country can be completed quickly. (26th Central News Agency Dispatch)

The National Labor Six Conventions Approved by the National Government

(Nanjing) According to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, the six draft conventions formulated by the International Labour Conference, including (1) Repatriation of Seafarers, (2) Minimum Age for Employment of Children at Sea, (3) Minimum Age for Employment of Stokers or Trimmers, (4) Conditions for Seafarers' Employment Agreements, (5) Compulsory Medical Examination for Employment of Children and Young People at Sea, and (6) Employment of Women Underground in All Mines, have now been approved by the National Government, and it has been decided to postpone approval of (1) Unemployment Compensation for Shipwreck or Loss, (2) Simplification of Emigration on Ships, and (3) Facilitating Seafarers' Employment. (26th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Calculation Method of Income Tax: Ministry of Finance Compiles Explanation and Orders Subordinates to Take Note; Also Stipulates the Scope of Public Officials

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance recently sent letters to various agencies across the country, stating that income tax on the salaries and remuneration of public officials has already been levied. However, there have been changes in this tax rate and progressive calculation method compared to the income donation previously collected by the Central Government. Regarding tax calculation, the "Calculation Table of Taxable Amount for Category II Income" and "Collection Instructions" were previously printed and distributed separately. Now, an explanation of the scope of public officials and the calculation method of their salary and remuneration income has been formulated and attached to the letter to make it easier for withholding agencies to understand. The main points of the explanation are as follows: 1. The scope of public officials is as follows: (1) Committee members and staff of party committees at all levels and their affiliated agencies; (2) Staff of central and local governments and their affiliated agencies; (3) Staff and teachers of national, provincial, municipal, and county schools; (4) Staff of government-operated enterprises; (5) Personnel of local autonomous organizations; (6) Other personnel engaged in public service in accordance with laws and regulations. 2. Laborers and workers in the aforementioned agencies are not public officials and should fall within the scope of other practitioners. 3. For public officials whose salary and remuneration income is calculated on a monthly basis, if the income is less than one month, the actual amount of income should be used to calculate the tax at the original tax rate. 4. If various agencies fail to pay full salaries on a monthly basis, taxes should be levied according to the following methods: (1) For those who receive discounted salaries, the tax should be calculated based on the actual amount issued first, and when the supplementary payment is made, it should be combined with the amount already issued to calculate and pay the supplementary tax; for those who use borrowing to replace salary payment, the actual amount borrowed each month should be used to calculate and pay the supplementary payment in accordance with the previous regulations. 5. If the salary and remuneration income is calculated on an annual basis, the total amount of income for one year should be divided by the number of months in a year, and the amount obtained should be the average amount per month. 6. If the income is periodic, the number of months in the period and the total amount of income should be averaged according to the previous method. 7. If the salary and remuneration income includes both monthly income and annual income, or periodic income, and there are more than two types, it should be combined and averaged. 8. In all cases involving items 3 to 7, the withholding agency should specify them separately in the withholding list when reporting. (26th Central News Agency Dispatch)

The Fourth Route Army Inspection Group Visits Military Academy

(Nanjing) All members of the Fourth Route Army's domestic military inspection group departed from their residence accompanied by reception personnel on the morning of the 26th to visit the military academy, and returned in the evening. Anti-Smuggling Committee May Not Confiscate Private Goods

(Nanjing) The Shantou Silk Industry Association previously established an anti-smuggling committee to prevent smuggling, and formulated measures to ban private goods, which were submitted to the Chaozhou Customs Superintendent for referral to the Ministry of Finance for record. It is now learned that the Ministry of Finance believes that the association's enthusiasm in assisting the government in anti-smuggling is commendable. However, the measures submitted for banning private goods, which include confiscating private goods and imposing fines, are beyond the scope of authority. Because the execution of confiscating private goods and imposing fines are both within the authority of the Customs. If various associations discover private goods or the purchase of private goods, they should immediately report to the Customs or assist the Customs in investigating and seizing them. They should not be allowed to handle it themselves. The registration of commercial goods should also comply with the "Provisional Regulations for Inspection of Imported Goods Transportation and Sales" previously promulgated. The Chaozhou Customs Superintendent has been ordered to revise it properly and notify the Customs Superintendents in its area to take note of it. (26th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Cause of Fire in Internal Library

(Nanjing) A fire broke out in the library of the Ministry of Interior at around 7:00 pm on the evening of the 25th. Three rooms were burned down. The national gazettes stored inside were the most precious. The cause of the fire was that the wires of the street lights in front of the library caught fire. Fortunately, the fire was extinguished in time, and it did not spread to the archives room, which can be said to be a blessing in disguise. The total amount of losses has not yet been calculated. Regarding the aftermath, Minister Jiang [Zuobin], in addition to ordering his subordinates to be more careful, also ordered them to inspect the wires and build a new library to store books and archives, so that this unfortunate event will not happen again. (26th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Chengdu and Chongqing (Part Two)

— Chang Qing

There have been many records of the scenery of Chengdu in newspapers and magazines. In short, it is very elegant and beautiful. The trees in public parks such as Shaocheng Park, Zhiji Stone Park, and Beicheng Park... are all tall and soaring in the air. Every household in the major streets and alleys plants a poplar, sycamore, locust, mulberry, cypress... or other trees in front of their doors to complement the scenery. There are even more gardens in private mansions. If you climb high and look out, the rooftops are covered with a lush green. Chengdu has originally been afforested. At sunset, it is simply a beautiful urban painting. Chongqing, on the other hand, has no better places to visit other than Nanwenquan and Beiwenquan. There are few trees in the city. The artificial scenery of the parks is not as natural as that of Chengdu. The land force of each family member seems to be like an invaded country, and the territory is shrinking very pitifully. The houses are mostly built several stories high, but this is not the residence of the general gentry class. Most of them are several families or dozens of families living together. Light is not easily revealed. It is so dark and humid. Living inside makes people feel suffocated. In summer, it is even hotter, making everyone feel uncomfortable. Compared to the climate, Chengdu is very gentle.

Although Chengdu is located in the westernmost corner of Sichuan, its material civilization is not lagging behind. Speaking of construction, it seems to be more advanced than Chongqing. The roads in Chengdu, whether major streets or alleys, were built flat and smooth for "East Ocean cars" [rickshaws] very early on. Chongqing is still building roads in the city. Because of the undulating terrain of the city, the transportation tool that is considered to be a thing of the past – sedan chairs – is still prevalent. However, judging from the authorities' efforts in construction, Chongqing is actually putting in more effort and developing faster than Chengdu. Chongqing's tap water pipes have been widely installed in every citizen's home, and the previously difficult problem of water use has now been completely resolved. The construction of houses is more elaborate than in Chengdu. New villages and municipal hospitals are also being planned. As for the rectification of the city appearance and the equipment of fire protection... these are indeed several times better than they were five years ago.

Since the slogan "Sichuan as the base for national rejuvenation" was put forward, many people from other provinces have let go and ran into Sichuan. Chengdu has also become more prosperous day by day along with Chongqing. Many new hotels, restaurants, and teahouses have been added, and entertainment venues are springing up like mushrooms after rain, even surpassing Chongqing in vigor. In the commercial center area designated as the Chengdu Special Zone, Chunxi Road Commercial Square, Zongfu Street, and Dongda Street are illuminated by neon lights at night, and the tourists are like weaving. All the shops are brazenly making enticing promotions. Gramophones and radios are turned on together to compete for business. The liveliness is no less than that of Chongqing. However, when asked about the real trade situation, it can be said that the doors may seem bustling, but there are few customers. This fully demonstrates the urban economy's external strength and internal weakness.

Letter Received

To the esteemed editors: I have just read in your newspaper today a Nanjing dispatch stating, "The National Association of Chinese Cotton Mill Owners has petitioned for urgent relief," and so on. Upon investigation, our association has not recently petitioned the government for relief. Upon careful examination of the reported items, they seem to be resolutions passed by the Chinese Textile Engineering Society four or five months ago, or matters submitted by that society to the central government for review, and thus mistakenly attributed to our association. We hereby request a correction. Respectfully request your attention to this matter. With best wishes for your well-being. Secretariat of the Chinese Cotton Mill Owners Association. October 26th, 25th year of the Republic.

Commentary

The Union of Italy and Germany and the Crisis in Europe

— Hua

The former Italian Foreign Minister Ciano visited Berlin the other day and met with the German leader Hitler and Foreign Minister Neurath, deciding on eight points of cooperation between the two countries in diplomacy. This so-called "cooperation," in its form and wording, seems to resolve the contradictions between the two countries and propel Europe towards "construction" and "peace." In reality, this is not the case. The union of Italy and Germany is merely a temporary compromise on the Austrian issue, changing from a competition for hegemony to a temporary agreement. In other areas, due to the "full cooperation" of these two fascist aggressor states, the crisis of peace in Europe will become increasingly severe.

Let us examine the eight points of cooperation between the two countries announced by Ciano. From the first to the fourth points, it can be said that they concern general diplomatic unity, that is, the two countries will adopt a unified stance on the Western European Pact countries, the League of Nations, and the Danube River issues. The fifth point concerns Spain, where the two countries express support for the fascist rebels who share their views. This shows that although they have not formally recognized the rebel government, recognition is imminent. The sixth and seventh points express their joint support for fascism and opposition to Bolshevism. The eighth concerns Germany's recognition of Italy's annexation of Abyssinia. In addition, it is said that there is another agreement, indicating that Italy agrees to support Germany's demand for the restoration of colonies. None of this is revealed.

In summary, these two countries, which are striving to overthrow the international status quo and expand their power abroad, have decided to mutually recognize their demands that hinder peace, and to adopt a unified hostile attitude towards the forces currently maintaining the status quo and upholding peace in the international community. For example, the so-called "promoting the Western European Pact" refers to Italy's support for Germany's position on the Locarno issue. Germany's recognition of Italy's annexation of Abyssinia is clearly a quid pro quo for Italy's support for Germany's recovery of colonies. As for the League of Nations, the only cornerstone of the current international peace system, the two countries have also decided on a unified strategy based on their shared opposition. Such so-called "full cooperation," if the beautiful rhetoric of "peace" and "construction" is removed, does not allow us to be optimistic about the future of the European situation.

Not only can we not be optimistic, but we will also feel that the current crisis in Europe is increasingly irreversible. The most obvious is the issue of Spain. The struggle between the Spanish rebels and the People's Front government over who is illegal and who is legal has long been judged by the international community. However, while democratic forces around the world sympathize with the legitimate government of Spain, Germany and Italy, solely because of their shared fascist sentiments and their ambitions in the Mediterranean and Africa, have disregarded the non-intervention agreement and vigorously aided the rebels in secret. Who is to blame for the bloodshed all over the Iberian Peninsula? Anyone with a sense of justice will understand. Now, Portugal, influenced by Germany and Italy, has formally severed diplomatic relations with the Madrid government and recognized the rebel government, as a prelude to Germany and Italy's recognition of the rebel government. The serious significance of this behavior, which violates international norms, cannot be ignored. Moreover, due to Germany and Italy's violation of the non-intervention agreement, the Soviet Union has also been forced to take free action. In the future, the development of conflicts in the Mediterranean will be unstoppable.

At this time, the response of Britain and France is extremely important. The People's Front in France was originally not strong enough in unity, but after this Radical Socialist Party congress, the internal divisions within the People's Front have been patched up, which is gratifying. However, France's foreign policy must be constrained by Britain. The stubbornness of the British Conservative government and the weakness and incompetence of the Labour Party have caused British foreign policy to waver between upholding the collective peace system and condoning fascist aggression. This flaw has not been remedied to this day. If the current crisis in Europe becomes more serious, even causing the final tragedy, the vacillating politicians of Britain will have to bear a great responsibility.

Thousands of Old and Young in Madrid Dig Trenches Along the Capital, Braving the Cold and Rain, as the Rebels Prepare for a Second General Offensive

Madrid: The government has advised all residents of the capital to dig trenches around the city to prevent the rebel advance. As a result, several thousand people, old and young, set out to work in the suburbs this morning, each carrying shovels and lunch boxes. Despite the rain and cold weather, they did not seem to mind. An uninformed observer would have thought they were on a holiday outing in the countryside. In addition, most of the young people belonging to various labor unions are taking advantage of their free time to conduct military exercises. This afternoon, more than 20,000 young workers marched in formation in the center of the capital. However, only a few of them carried rifles. Residents of the city generally expressed optimism, believing that everyone would soon be able to obtain weapons to fight. They also believed that although rebel aircraft occasionally threatened the capital, the government would soon obtain fighter planes to defend against enemy air raids. According to general opinion, the labor unions could supply 40,000 to 50,000 strong men to the front lines if necessary. Also, at 4:30 this afternoon, several rebel aircraft soared in the sky over the capital, but they flew very high and soon left. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

Barcelona: At 10 AM today, four workers' organizations in Barcelona held a mass meeting at the city's bullring. Ten thousand people participated, and the atmosphere was very enthusiastic. The workers' organizations belonging to various parties and factions in Barcelona jointly agreed on Thursday of last week to unite against foreign aggression. Therefore, a mass meeting was convened today to announce this. Representatives from various workers' organizations gave speeches, calling on workers to sacrifice everything for the war. Workers had obtained the right to a 40-hour work week and a 15% wage increase on July 15th of this year. Due to the urgency of the war, workers should temporarily give up this right. Next, a representative of the Catalan Autonomous Government reported on the results of last night's government meetings. The meeting decided to mobilize people of all classes, confiscate all civilian firearms, and convert all industries to a "collective production" system. The meeting then adjourned in cheers. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

Darafanra: A special dispatch from our reporter. People in the National Army Command on the front lines here now believe that the city of Madrid is within easy reach. It will fall within three days at the earliest, and ten days at the latest. The only unknown is how to capture it. In general, General Franco's troops are in high spirits, with sharp weapons, and victory is assured. There is no need to make unnecessary sacrifices to achieve a quick victory. General Franco himself does not want to bombard the capital fiercely to avoid the suffering of the people. Therefore, he will leave a lifeline for the residents of the capital, allowing them to escape the encirclement to the port of Valencia in the east. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

(London) The Spanish National Revolutionary Army will issue a general attack order on Madrid in a few hours. According to General Varela, a leader of the National Army, Madrid will be occupied by Thursday of this week. The National Army acknowledges that it suffered a setback in the area of Pimi Linoz, but claims that after the government forces counterattacked Lasna, Vas, and Talmax, they were stopped from advancing. At present, Naval Piral is in fierce fighting. According to officials of the National Army, the army suffered a slight setback at the beginning of the attack, but soon turned defeat into victory, and Escorial will fall imminently. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

Darafanra: The cavalry, tank, and artillery units led by Colonel Monnais de Ria of the National Army have surrounded the city of Alanyus. Alanyus is located on a high mountain with steep cliffs, making it a strategic point for guarding the capital of Madrid. After the city falls, the final decisive battle to attack Madrid will begin. Currently, all units of the National Army are deployed on the southern and western sides of the capital. As soon as the order is given, they can pounce forward. General Mullah, the commander-in-chief of the entire front, arrived in the city of Dolius this month to discuss everything with General Varela, the commander of the colonial army. According to recent reports, General Varela has contributed the most to the National Army's capture of various fortresses around the capital. However, the colonial army's organization is not unified, and it lacks the effect of coordinated assistance. Therefore, it is generally expected that an order will be issued tomorrow to adjust the command of the various armies on the front lines and to delineate the battle lines of each army separately before a general attack can begin. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

Escorial Rebel Front Line

The Spanish rebels advanced seven miles towards Madrid in the past two days, as if entering a no-man's land. Although the rugged mountains and rocks along the way could be used by the government forces to defend, the rebel advance only encountered a small number of government forces, artillery, and machine gun resistance. The left wing of the rebels has reached the area of Bigrino, while the rebels in Nova Telmark are dancing and making merry in the streets with a group of young girls. (National News dispatch, 26th)

Valtermoro Government Forces Front Line: The town of Xinpu Ruiluo, 17 miles from Madrid, was evacuated in panic today, but the militia remained to defend the town and prevent the rebel advance. Government forces and rebels are currently engaged in fierce artillery battles, and rebels are bombing the town with aircraft. (National News dispatch, 25th)

(London) Spanish rebel General Talano officially announced on the Cesal radio station today that the government forces' attempt to recapture Illesca had been repelled, with 300 killed and 100 captured, including Golell, a reporter for the Associated Press. Talano said that after Golell confirmed that he was a reporter, he was treated with courtesy. However, Mini Fee, a reporter for the New York Tribune, and Weaver, a reporter for the London News Chronicle, have been missing since this morning after leaving Madrid for the front lines. Nava Hong, the driver of the Associated Press reporter, returned to the capital alone after Golell was captured, saying that they arrived at Vol de Moro at 1 PM. It was said that they could travel three kilometers south, but they still saw nothing upon reaching their destination. He repeatedly urged Nava not to go any further, but he refused to listen and continued for five kilometers in a car full of soldiers. Suddenly, they encountered a rebel tank, which opened fire with a machine gun. Golell immediately jumped into a small ditch, while the driver turned the car around. When the tank approached, Golell took out the American flag hidden in his sleeve, which saved him from being crushed to death. The area is on the highway between Madrid and Alandus, only 17 miles south of Madrid. (National News dispatch, 26th)

Lisbon: According to unconfirmed reports today, plans for the Spanish government to abandon Madrid have been completed. It is also heard that 82 rebel aircraft flew over Madrid today, distributing leaflets warning the government to surrender to avoid bloodshed. (National News dispatch, 26th)

Lisbon: According to the Lisbon Daily News, two large aircraft parked at the Madrid airfield, preparing to carry Western government officials to a safe area when the rebels launched their final offensive, have reportedly been destroyed by bombing by National Army aircraft. Rebel aircraft also reported that a giant bomber, en route to the rebel headquarters in Burgos, presumably to bomb the town, had been shot down and destroyed. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

Portugal Refutes Soviet Russia, Says It is Inciting Internal Strife

(London) Portugal's response to the Soviet Union's accusation that the country is aiding the Spanish rebels has been submitted to the Non-Intervention Committee. The original text has been published today. The rebuttal states that the Soviet Union has attempted to incite a communist revolution in Portugal and provoke war between Portugal and Spain. Soviet Ambassador to Spain Rosenberg has effectively controlled the Madrid government and recently secretly convened Madrid communists to elect Gabalello as prime minister. Soviet officers are currently planning the defense of Madrid, and dozens of Soviet airmen with chemicals have arrived at the Getterfield airfield in Madrid. The note further states that a Soviet Union is "striving to achieve victory in the first war it has created." The Portuguese note then refutes the Soviet Union's accusation, stating that Portugal must purchase foreign arms to strengthen its national defense. Therefore, it is unfounded to accuse Portugal of supplying arms to the Spanish rebels. (National News dispatch, 25th)

US Communist Party Leader's Speech Interrupted and Expelled

Denver, USA: US Communist Party presidential candidate Browder was giving a speech here today when a group calling themselves "Red-Blooded Americans" stormed the stage, expelled Browder, and injured 12 members of the audience. Browder was speaking in an open space to an audience of 400 people when suddenly someone shouted, "Red-Blooded Americans, those of you who cannot tolerate this, come quickly!" Before the shout had ended, about 20 men wearing American veterans' hats, each holding pistols and iron weapons, rushed into the crowd, injuring 12 people and tearing off the clothes of three people. They went to the stage, tore up flags, and overturned the stage. By this time, Browder had escaped into a small grove. Later, he told an Associated Press reporter in a hotel that six audience members were receiving medical treatment for injuries, and three women had been knocked to the ground, but only suffered minor injuries. Although Browder repeatedly asked the audience not to resist, the women scratched the faces of the thugs, and the men threw mud. Browder also said that he had repeatedly requested police protection, but to no avail. One of the thugs was even a special police officer. Browder will now file a lawsuit with the prosecutor. (National News dispatch, 25th)

Securities

For example, the decline in automobile and steel stocks was strong. Copper mining stocks fell in price following the announcement that production had increased to 95% of production capacity. New Record for China's Cotton Production This Year

(Washington) The US Department of Agriculture today released a report from its Shanghai-based commissioner, Dawson, stating that China produced 3.65 million bales of cotton this year, each bale weighing 500 pounds, setting a new record. The estimates for the minor provinces are still low. The weather was very good during the harvest, so this amount is likely to increase in the future. The increase in China's cotton production this year is largely due to the expansion of cotton-growing areas. In most places, however, the quality of cotton is lower than last year. Although this year's harvest is abundant, cotton prices in China are very high. Only 80% of the yarn factories run by Chinese in the country are operating, while all of the yarn factories run by Japanese are operating. (National News dispatch, 25th)

The Balkan Entente and the Little Entente Discuss Military Mutual Assistance Measures; Yugoslavia Will Follow in Germany's Footsteps and Recognize Italy's Annexation of Abyssinia

Capital of Romania: According to well-informed sources, the chiefs of staff of the armies of Romania, Yugoslavia, Greece, and Turkey, countries of the Balkan and Little Ententes, will come here with their assistants and experts on November 3 to gather and discuss. According to military sources, the purpose of the meeting is to establish the foundation of a mutual aid group, so that if one of the four Entente countries is attacked, the other three countries should come to its aid. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

Capital of Yugoslavia: The 29th of this month is the anniversary of Turkey's National Day. The Prime Minister and Foreign Minister of Yugoslavia, Stojadinović, left this morning from here to the capital of Turkey for this purpose. He will meet with President Kemal of that country. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

Capital of Yugoslavia: According to well-informed sources in this city, the Yugoslav government will announce its recognition of Italy's annexation of Abyssinia within days. In effect, this means that Yugoslavia is joining the sphere of influence of Italy and Germany. Germany was the first to recognize Abyssinia as part of the Italian Empire. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

The Locarno Question: The Content of Belgium's Reply; The Expansion of Armies by Various Countries Threatens Belgium; The Franco-Belgian Alliance is Sufficient Grounds for Justification

Regarding the question of convening a future Locarno conference, the Belgian government submitted a reply to the British government's note of September 18th on Friday of last week (the 23rd), and it was delivered to the Foreign Office by the country's ambassador to Britain, Mashian. It is understood that its content explains the country's new position in diplomacy after King Leopold III's recent declaration of neutrality. It states that since the countries have been sparing no effort in strengthening their armies, the effectiveness of the Locarno Treaty in guaranteeing Belgium's security has been greatly reduced, and the risk of Belgium suffering foreign aggression has greatly increased. The reason why Belgium has adopted a new policy is precisely this. The Locarno Treaty stipulates that the signatory countries should collectively maintain the current state of the territories of European countries. This obligation was originally extremely important for small countries like Belgium. However, at that time, Germany's armaments had been withdrawn, the Rhineland had been designated a demilitarized zone, and the power of the League of Nations was still substantial. Therefore, the effectiveness of the Locarno Treaty in guaranteeing Belgium's security was still more than sufficient. This is precisely the reason why Belgium ratified this treaty. Since then, first, Germany rearmed, and then disputes arose between Italy and Abyssinia, weakening the authority of the League of Nations. In addition, France is pursuing a policy of alliance, and European countries are in danger of being divided into two major groups confronting each other. The times have changed, and the situation is as such. After the French and Belgian general staffs concluded a technical cooperation agreement, the defensive fortifications built by Belgium will inevitably be regarded by Germany as an extension of France's eastern "Maginot Line." Therefore, if France and Germany were to clash, Belgian territory would undoubtedly be invaded. If so, Belgium might be annihilated before the guarantor countries of the Locarno Treaty could come to its aid. In short, if Belgium can act in a way that gives other countries no excuse to invade its territory, the security of Western Europe, especially the security of Britain, will be enhanced. After Belgium's above-mentioned reply was delivered, the British Cabinet will study it within this week. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

Talks Between Italy and Germany Will Continue in the Future

Munich: Regarding the discussions of Foreign Minister Ciano of Italy and other important Italian personnel during their stay in Leed, an authoritative source issued a statement today, stating that the talks between Italy and Ciano and German Prime Minister Hitler and important German personnel involved all current political, economic, and social issues of importance that are directly related to the two countries. The atmosphere was extremely friendly and sincere. As a result of the exchange of views, agreement was reached on all important issues. Both governments attach importance to advocating international peace and rebuilding normal life in the international community. In order to implement all resolutions, both governments are willing to continue contacts. (National News dispatch, 25th)

(Rome) Count Ciano, the Minister of Foreign Affairs, went to Germany for consultation and held talks with German leader Hitler in the city of Berchtesgaden. Afterward, he was able to travel to the city of Siena, where he was given a grand welcome by the local authorities and the public. He has now completed his public duties and returned here by plane from Siena at 1:15 PM today. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

Austrian Foreign Minister Arrives in Hungary to Discuss German-Italian Relations

Budapest, Hungary - Following Hungarian Foreign Minister Kánya's visit to Austria in September of this year, Austrian Foreign Minister Guido Schmidt arrived here from Vienna at 11:00 AM today to return the visit. Schmidt is scheduled to meet with Prime Minister Darányi and Foreign Minister Kánya this afternoon, and will be received by Regent Horthy on Wednesday before returning to Vienna. Well-informed sources suggest that Schmidt's visit is to discuss the impact of the recent talks in Berlin between German and Italian officials on Central Europe, as well as the future of the proposed Vienna conference between Italy, Austria, and Hungary. It is noted that these three countries have expressed their willingness to allow other nations to join the Rome Protocols previously signed by them. Furthermore, Czech Prime Minister Hodza recently declared that Central European countries could use the Little Entente as a foundation for larger collaborative efforts. This indicates that Schmidt's visit is motivated by the more compromising attitude of Hungary's current Prime Minister Darányi compared to his predecessor Gömbös, and aims to seize this opportunity to negotiate the inclusion of other nations in the Rome Protocols. (Havas, 26th)

Automatic Physician

(London) At the London Medical Exhibition, which closed last week, an "automatic physician" was displayed for the first time. This device cannot actually diagnose a patient's ailments but is a machine that, when rolled over the body, indicates on a dial the points where disease-causing organisms are concentrated in the blood. (Special dispatch from the North-China Daily News, 25th)

Belgian Fascist Party's Plan to March on the Capital Fails; Arrested Members Gradually Released; Heated Debate at Socialist Party Congress

Brussels - The Rexist Party's plan to "march" on Brussels has clearly failed completely. Today, the police were able to maintain order without resorting to force. Rexist Party members who gathered in various locations were dispersed by the police, and over 250 people were arrested. Except for important figures in the party, the rest were released after brief questioning. The party's Secretary-General, Yvan Hallux, issued a statement to the press, stating that "Our party leader, Léon Degrelle, is still detained by the police, but the charges against him are still unknown. We only know that he requested paper and pen from the police to write his first article from prison for the party's newspaper. Others arrested with Degrelle include Member of Parliament Canape and Senator Count de Thiennes. Count de Thiennes was allegedly mistreated by the police. The party has scheduled a meeting tonight to elect an interim leader to 'replace Degrelle.'" The Rexist Party also issued a statement strongly protesting the arrest of its leader, Degrelle, stating that the party will continue to respect the law and calling on the nation to "denounce the red dictatorship and Soviet-style violence." In addition, Justice Minister Bovesse told a reporter from this agency, "The government is determined to maintain order throughout the country, and any disruptive behavior, regardless of its origin, will be punished. Rexist Party leader Degrelle is inciting the public by claiming a communist threat. Some people are misled by him and become alarmed. It should be known that the government firmly opposes dictatorship of any kind. The majority of the people support the government, and the government will adopt a firm and moderate policy to maintain public support. The government is responsible for maintaining order and will not allow anyone to interfere." (Havas, 25th)

Brussels - People here were anticipating a bloody Sunday, as over 250,000 Belgian Fascist party members were expected to hold a demonstration against the government's orders. However, they were pleasantly surprised that today passed peacefully. Most of the troublemakers did not appear. It is reported that although several groups of Belgian Fascist party members gathered in the streets and clashed with police, resulting in over 200 arrests, the crimes committed by the party members were merely disobeying police orders and refusing to move. Overall, yesterday passed peacefully, with only one Socialist party member being shot in the foot by a Fascist in front of the party headquarters, and two police officers receiving minor injuries while dispersing Fascists, and are currently being treated in the hospital. (Reuters, 25th)

Brussels - Following yesterday's arrest of Fascist Rexist Party leader Léon Degrelle and over 200 party members for holding demonstrations, in addition to the release of a batch last night, all the important figures were also released this morning. Some party members held demonstrations in the city center last night, but the momentum was weak and they were dispersed by the police. The situation in the capital has now returned to normal. The general impression is that Degrelle and the Rexist Party's two demonstrations have suffered a major defeat. (Havas, 26th)

Brussels - The Socialist Party is currently holding a congress here. Minister without Portfolio Vandervelde will present a report on the international situation, mentioning the Spanish problem, stating, "Portugal has now severed diplomatic relations with the Spanish government. The future of the international situation is extremely serious. All countries participating in the non-intervention agreement should reconsider the Spanish situation. As a member of the Belgian government, I am bound by the decisions of the government, but as the leader of the Belgian Socialist Party, I dare say that the aid our party is willing to give to Spain does not violate the decision to ban arms shipments. Money and clothing can be sent to Spain." (Havas, 25th)

Brussels - At the Socialist Party congress yesterday, Foreign Minister Spaak and Minister without Portfolio Vandervelde disagreed and engaged in a heated debate. There is no other choice." Vandervelde then retorted, "If I had to choose between Fascism and Bolshevism, I would rather choose Bolshevism." (Havas, 26th)

French Radical Party Issues Declaration, Congress Concludes

Biarritz - The Radical Socialist Party Congress, which lasted for four days, concluded at noon today with the singing of the national anthem. The final decision-making session this morning was purely focused on the internal organization of the party. At the closing ceremony, a congress declaration was read, summarizing the key points of the resolutions passed yesterday, namely: (1) the occupation of factories by workers must stop; (2) support for the policy of non-intervention in the Spanish Civil War; (3) a desire to restore budgetary balance; (4) unwavering commitment to the League of Nations covenant and alliances with other countries; (5) approval of the actions taken by the Radical Socialist Party members in the Popular Front cabinet. The majority of delegates at the congress expressed support for the resolutions and the declaration. Delegates opposed to the Communist Party believed that the congress had appropriately denounced the occupation of factories by workers and the Communist Party's advocacy of intervention in the Spanish Civil War, which was highly satisfactory. Those who supported the Popular Front stated that the congress had endorsed the actions taken by the Radical Socialist Party members in the cabinet, allowing those cabinet members to continue to cooperate with Prime Minister Léon Blum and the Socialist Party cabinet members. After the adjournment, a grand banquet was held. At the end of the banquet, party leader and Minister of National Defense Daladier delivered a speech, stating that "All attempts by fascism have been eliminated due to the existence of the Popular Front. It would be absurd for our party to promote the breakup of the Popular Front at this time, but there can be no social justice if the entire nation cannot live together peacefully and respect order. And the Popular Front cannot succeed if it cannot protect the democratic interests of the entire nation. This is what our party should announce to the entire nation." (Havas, 25th)

Romanian Parties Demonstrate, Expressing Three Trends

Bucharest, Romania - The government's Liberal Party, the opposition National Peasant Party, and the far-right Romanian Front held separate demonstrations yesterday, expressing three trends of public opinion. The main points of the speeches by key figures of each party are summarized below:

(1) The Liberal Party held a gathering in Turnu Severin, where party leader and State Counselor Gheorghe Tătărescu delivered a speech, reiterating his support for the League of Nations and advocating for maintaining friendly relations with the Soviet Union, provided that the Soviet Union does not interfere in Romania's internal affairs.

Romania's friendly relations with the Soviet Union should also be promoted, provided that the Soviet Union does not interfere in Romania's internal affairs. (3) The far-right Romanian Front held a gathering in Craiova, where the Front's Secretary-General and former Deputy Secretary-General of the State Council, Tira, delivered a speech, advocating that the government should find ways to limit the continued increase in the Jewish population. Paris to Saigon Air Race of 12,000 Miles; Three Take Off, One Returns

(Paris) - The 13,000-mile air race from Paris to Saigon began today. Three planes participated. One, piloted by Charles and Brier, took off from Le Bourget Airport at 6:00 AM, but soon returned to repair the engine. It took off again at 8:33 AM and landed in Lyon at 4:25 PM, then flew to Turin. After arriving there, it decided to withdraw from the race due to a broken oil pipe. The other two planes, one piloted by Arnoux and Yobi, landed safely in Athens and then departed from Baghdad at 6:50 PM. Baghdad is a mandatory stop. The other, piloted by Testot-Troyat and Delmotte, was forced to land in Corinth due to a lack of fuel. Fortunately, the plane was not damaged. After refueling, it continued to fly to Tatoi and should arrive there tomorrow. The only other mandatory stop on the route is Karachi. (Reuters, 26th)

(Paris) - Among the aviators participating in the long-distance round-trip flight competition between Paris and Saigon, the Arnoux and Yobi team is currently in the lead, followed by the Testot-Troyat and Delmotte team. The Charles and Brier team has abandoned the race midway. The details are as follows:

The Arnoux and Yabi team flew over Brindisi, Italy, at 3:05 PM and arrived in Greece at the Tatoi airfield at 3:40 PM. They stayed for one hour and ten minutes and resumed flying at 4:50 PM. By 8:10 PM, they had flown between Rhodes and Cyprus in the Mediterranean Sea.

The Testot-Troyat and Delmotte team flew over the Greek island of Corfu in the Mediterranean Sea at 1:05 PM and arrived at the Tatoi airfield at 3:05 PM. Later, due to running out of gasoline, they were forced to land near Corinth, Greece. They immediately reported to Paris by long-distance telephone, saying, "The weather was very bad when we flew over the Adriatic Sea. Thin ice formed on the wings, reducing our speed and delaying us for an hour and a half. Later, we ran out of gasoline and had to land near Corinth. We are now waiting for gasoline. If we can find it, we will continue flying tomorrow." Athens dispatched a truck full of gasoline to the landing site at 8:00 PM to supply Testot-Troyat and others.

The Charles and Brier team, after flying to Turin, Italy, had to fly back to Lyon, France, and land at 4:25 PM due to engine damage on the right side and were unable to continue flying. They decided to abandon the competition and will fly back to Paris tomorrow to repair the engine. (Havas, 25th)

Baghdad - In the Paris-Saigon air race, the plane piloted by Arnoux and Yobi arrived here at 12:48 last night and then flew to the mandatory stop of Karachi at 1:45 this morning. The two flew 3,200 miles in 16 hours and 30 minutes after leaving Le Bourget Airport yesterday morning. The plane piloted by Testot-Troyat and Delmotte was forced to land due to a lack of fuel. Fortunately, the plane was not damaged and is currently en route to Tatoi. (Reuters, 26th)

Details of the Assassination of Chairman Yang Yongtai of Hubei Province: Shot Twice, Died in Hospital; Assailant Apprehended on the Spot; Funeral Committee Formed to Handle Aftermath; Secretary Lu Zhu Acts as Chairman

Hankou Dispatch, 25th - An assassination occurred in Hankou today. The victim was Yang Yongtai, Chairman of Hubei Province and Secretary-General of the Military Affairs Commission Chairman's Headquarters. He was shot twice and died of his wounds after 22 minutes. The assailant was apprehended on the spot. The details are as follows:

Circumstances of the Assassination on the Riverfront

Yang Yongtai, accompanied by his wife, crossed the Yangtze River from Wuchang to Hankou at 1:00 PM on the 25th to attend a banquet hosted by the American consul. After the banquet at 3:00 PM, he, his wife, and an attendant crossed the river back to the provincial government. Due to strong winds, the ferry could not operate, so they switched to the Wuhan ferry. At 3:15 PM, they arrived at Pier 1 in front of the Jianghan Customs House in Hankou in their private car number 488. As they alighted from the car, an assailant suddenly appeared and fired three shots at Yang's back. Yang was hit by two bullets, but remained conscious and tried to remain calm, intending to return to Wuchang. Supported by his wife, he boarded the car and was rushed to Tongren Hospital in Special District 1 for treatment. He arrived at the hospital at 3:27 PM. Yang was still able to get out of the car and speak. The hospital director, Fujita, and doctors examined him and found that two bullets had entered from the lower part of the right back between the shoulder blades, and one bullet had passed through the lower part of the right rib. One bullet remained in the upper part of the sixth rib. Two injections of cardiac stimulant were administered. However, due to the severity of the injuries, he died at 3:37 PM.

Assailant Apprehended on the Spot

The assailant was a young man. When Yang was shot, there was chaos on the riverfront. The police officer on duty apprehended the assailant. The assailant resisted. Pedestrians ran for cover. A stray bullet injured a woman. When the police officer on duty blew his whistle wildly, other police officers arrived and apprehended the assailant on the spot. He was initially detained at the 6th Public Security Bureau and then transferred to the Public Security Bureau, and then to the Wuhan Garrison Headquarters, where Commander Chen Jicheng personally interrogated him. The assailant's name is Chen Xiechao, a native of Sichuan, 20 years old, residing in rooms 56 and 14 at the Jinghan Hotel in the French Concession. Today, he took a rickshaw from somewhere to the Jianghan Customs House, waited for about half an hour, and fired at Yang when he got out of the car. The assailant has been apprehended on the spot, and it is believed that further information will be readily obtained.

Funeral Committee Formed by All Sectors

When Yang entered the hospital, He Chengjun, Chen Jicheng, and all members and directors of the provincial government came to the hospital to express their condolences. However, Yang had already passed away. At 4:10 PM, the body was moved to the Bank Association building. Leaders of various institutions and groups, foreign consuls and military attachés came to pay their respects and view the remains. Yang's body lay on a couch, wearing a blue robe and black mandarin jacket, still in the formal attire he wore to the banquet. His wife was overcome with grief and fainted once, but recovered after medical treatment. That evening, a funeral committee was formed by all sectors, and Lu Zhu, member and secretary-general of the provincial government, was appointed as the director. Sixty committee members were appointed, including Yu Yuzhi, Wang Shaoyou, Yang Jinyu, Liu Minggao, Ma Yuchen, Yang Zifu, Tao Yaojie, Zhang Daomin, Zai Shiliu, Jiang Shuzhi, Chen Lesan, Xie Chengbing, Xie Zhengyu, Zhang Yikun, Hu Guoting, Chen Guangzu, Cao Shijie, Li Boren, Liu Zushun, Chen Duzhen, Jin Zhenwei, Meng Guangpeng, Jia Shiyi, Cheng Qibao, Liu Shupeng, Li Shucheng, Fan Xiji, Wu Guozhen, Lu Zhu, Ding Bingquan, Jin Chentang, Shen Cheng, Huang Xi, Ling Hongxun, Huang Weicai, Chen Fang, Yu Huancheng, Chen Xizeng, Cai Mengjian, Cheng Wenxun, Xu Jishi, Xu Jizhuang, Nan Kui, Hong Yanbin, Xing Yaoshen, Huang Zhumin, Yi Cigan, Guan Tang, Tong Binqiu, Zhang [missing name], Huang Wenzhi, He Hengfu, Su Taiyu, Wang Daoping, Zhou Xingtang, Li Yaoqing, Wang Yaming, Liu Jingxian, Liu Bingyi, and Liu Jingzai. Ding Wenan. The committee was divided into six groups: (1) Documents Group: Lu Zhu, Chen Fang, Huang Zixian, Ye Jialong, Yu Jingtao, Deng Xiangyu, Ji Shiying, Guan Dazhong; (2) Decoration Group: Liu Shupeng, Hong Yanbin, Yi Cigan, Xu Jishi, He Hengfu; (3) General Affairs Group: Meng Guangpeng, Jia Bao, Wu Yue, Tong Binqiu, Chen Xiaoping, Wu Guo, Huang Zhumin, Chen Duzhen, Peng Shuyou, Wang Yufen, Zhou Liangdong; (4) Accounting Group: Jia Shiyi, Nan Kui, Zhou Qian, Deng Junzhi, Feng Zihui, Li Rulong; (5) Reception Group: Wu Guozhen, Cheng Qibao, Li Shucheng, Zhang Xiang, Guo Taizhen, Liu Bingyi, Liu Jingkun, Huang Wenzhi, Zai Jixi, Chen Zhiyuan, Feng Shaoyan; (6) Security Group: Jin Jutang, Chen Xizeng, Shen Cheng, Yang Zhen, Cai Mengjian, Huang Younan. Telegrams were sent to Shanghai to request that his family come to Hankou. The funeral home was also contacted to send someone by plane to inject preservative fluid into the body on the 26th. The body was placed in a coffin at the Bank Association building that day.

Provincial Committee Emergency Meeting

Yang's death caused shock in Wuhan. Lu Zhu, member and secretary-general of the provincial government, Meng Guangpeng, director of the Department of Civil Affairs, Jia Shiyi, director of the Department of Finance, Cheng Qibao, director of the Department of Education, Wu Guozhen, mayor of Hankou, and member Li Shucheng held an emergency meeting that evening. It was decided to report to the Central Government and Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, and to handle the funeral arrangements. Until the Central Government issues an official announcement regarding the successor as chairman, Lu Zhu, member and secretary-general of the provincial government, will serve as acting chairman, and provincial affairs will continue as usual. The public was also notified that anyone who fabricates rumors or disrupts public order will be arrested and prosecuted. (25th)

Photograph of Yang Yongtai After Death

Hubei Province Suffers Disaster in Forty-Seven Counties, Agricultural Losses Reach Ten Million "Dan," Autumn Drought Situation Severe

Hankou Correspondence: This year, various counties relied on rainfall for regulation, and both spring and autumn agricultural harvests and plantings were abundant. Since the beginning of autumn, for more than two months, there has been a severe drought with no rain, and autumn crops have withered. At the same time, reports of floods, wind disasters, and insect plagues have also been heard. The total losses due to disasters, according to available investigations, affect forty-seven counties. Among them, twenty-nine counties suffered from drought, five counties suffered from floods, twenty-three counties suffered from wind disasters, six counties suffered from pests and diseases, and ten counties suffered from other disasters. According to estimates by agricultural authorities, the affected area (in units of 100 "Shi Mu") is: wheat 81.923 "Mu," loss of 47.751 "Dan" (in units of 100 "Shi Dan"); barley 59.346 "Mu," loss of 31.721 "Dan"; peas 23.501 "Mu," loss of 13.768 "Dan"; broad beans 25.783 "Mu," loss of 24.418; oats 4 "Mu," loss of 0.001 "Dan," totaling 190.557 "Mu" with a loss of 117.659 "Dan" of agricultural products. Within the above disasters: drought affected 3.875 "Mu," with a loss of 2.411 "Dan"; floods affected 80.449 "Mu," with a loss of 52.060 "Dan"; wind disasters affected 72.918 "Mu," with a loss of 42.233 "Dan"; pests and diseases affected 5.32 "Mu," with a loss of 3.420 "Dan"; and other disasters affected 28.004 "Mu," with a loss of 17.535 "Dan." The total loss of agricultural products has reached more than ten million "Dan," with the autumn drought being particularly severe, which is truly unexpected. The provincial government, recognizing the disaster, is planning relief measures, and the soaring food prices are also affecting people's livelihoods. The planned Food Regulation Committee is expected to be established soon. (24th)

Soviet Ship Illegally Enters Magong Port, Japanese Navy Greatly Alarmed, Considering It Espionage, Taiwan Court Sentences Fine of 1,500 Yuan

Xiamen Correspondence: Magong Military Port in the Penghu Islands of Taiwan is the central base for the Japanese Navy in Taiwan and the South Seas and is highly valued. From June of last year to February of this year, foreign ships have illegally entered the Magong fortress area seven times under the pretext of seeking shelter from the wind. The Japanese Navy considers this to be organized international espionage. However, the court's investigation and trial concluded that there was insufficient evidence of espionage, and only fines were imposed for violations of ship laws. In February of this year, after discussions between the Japanese Naval Ministry and the Taiwan Governor-General's Office, it was announced that the opening of Magong Commercial Port would be abolished (Magong originally had separate commercial and military ports). On July 1st, the status of Magong as a foreign trade port was canceled, and foreign ships were absolutely prohibited from approaching Magong. Even domestic ships were not allowed to enter or leave, in order to completely prevent reconnaissance of the Magong Military Port. Unexpectedly, the Soviet ship "Tilik" (3,500 tons) departed from Nikolaev, European Russia, on June 28th, bound for Vladivostok in the Far East. After passing through Port Said, Aden, Colombo, and Singapore, it arrived at the Penghu Channel at 8:00 AM on August 16th. At 10:15 AM, at the location of 119 degrees 55 minutes East longitude and 23 degrees 378 minutes North latitude, it entered the Magong Military Port due to engine trouble, anchoring at Wukan Cape on Penghu Island, intruding into the fortress area by 1.9 nautical miles from the open sea. The Magong Naval Base Command immediately detained the ship and arrested the captain. Military police conducted a serious investigation, considering it an act of espionage. For a time, the Japanese naval community and Japanese residents in Taiwan were extremely agitated, calling it a "strange Soviet ship incident that threatened the Empire's national defense and shocked the world." This was because, after the closure of Magong Port, at a time of tense Russo-Japanese relations and Russia's plans to strengthen its Far East fleet, it attracted great attention from the Japanese. The case was then transferred to the Kaohsiung District Court for handling. As a result of the investigation, the captain was prosecuted, stating, "The defendant claimed to have entered to avoid a maritime accident due to engine failure and hull cracking. However, given the rising tide, switching engines and using the 'You Shu method' could have achieved its purpose without the need to anchor. Furthermore, there was the nearby open commercial port of Keelung, but the 'Tirak She' traveled backwards for several hours to enter the unopened Penghu, making the action very incomprehensible and suggesting espionage. At this time of international emergency, openly entering a known military port and fortress, we request a fine of 2,000 yuan and confiscation of the ship." After three public trials, the Soviet Consul-General in Kobe came to Taiwan to handle the case. The captain strongly denied any intention of espionage, and the Japanese lawyer hired to defend him also stated that it was only a violation of ship laws, and the so-called espionage was merely suspicion, with no sufficient evidence. On October 16th, the Kaohsiung District Court pronounced the verdict, finding the captain guilty of violating ship laws and "sentencing the captain to a fine of 1,500 yuan; if he cannot pay, he will be sentenced to 200 days of detention in lieu of the fine." The captain appeared satisfied in court, but did not state whether he would serve the sentence or appeal. If neither the prosecutor nor the defendant appeals, the incident can be concluded. However, the Japanese Navy remains indignant. (October 23rd)

Wujiang: Urging Payment of Airplane Birthday Celebration Funds

The Jiangsu Provincial Aviation Association stipulated that the local Chamber of Commerce should solicit 6,250 yuan for airplane birthday celebration donations. Now that Chairman Chiang's birthday is approaching, the local Chamber of Commerce has only raised 1,000 yuan. Kunshan: Planning to Build Sewers

The waterways in the urban area of ​​this county are divergent. Residents and shops arbitrarily dump garbage into the rivers, causing the riverbeds to become shallower and the water flow to stagnate. The water drawn for drinking is a breeding ground for diseases. The county government has decided to build sewers to discharge fresh water outside the city, which has been comprehensively planned by the Third Section in cooperation with the public servants' labor service team.

Suzhou: Zhouzhuang Township Robbery and Murder

The Wuxian District Court Prosecutor's Office reported, based on a report from the headman of Yaoyi Village, Huxi Township, Zhouzhuang Town, that seven or eight robbers dressed in gray cloth uniforms and armed with rifles and Mauser pistols broke into the home of Sun Yaowen on the 25th to commit robbery. Sun Yaowen attempted to resist and was shot and killed by the robbers. The losses were minimal. The robbers fled towards Taihu Lake. The court dispatched Prosecutor Lu and officials to the township for inspection on the 26th. It was confirmed that Sun Yaowen had indeed been shot and killed before his death. His brother Yaozhang was instructed to prepare a coffin for burial, and the perpetrators were being pursued and investigated.

Wuxi: Fierce Battle with Bandits in the Middle of the Night

Zhu Dingshen, the town head of Ganlu Town in the Eighth District, lived in Dongmao Village, Songzhi Township, and possessed assets. At about 10 PM the day before yesterday, more than a dozen bandits suddenly arrived, each wielding a weapon, and climbed over the wall to enter the premises. They frightened the men and women of the Zhu family into silence, tied them up with ropes, and then ransacked the house, searching for valuables at will. At that time, Police Chief Xu Shi of the town patrol station was patrolling with Runhua and others when they heard about the robbery. They went forward to pursue the bandits. The bandit on guard fired the first shot, but missed. The police then returned fire. The sound of gunfire echoed incessantly for more than ten minutes. The bandits were unable to hold out and fled. After the incident, the losses were counted to be more than 800 yuan. Yesterday, the Dangkou Public Security Seventh Branch reported the situation to the General Bureau and is strictly pursuing the escaped bandits.

Expanding Anti-Drug Propaganda

The county party headquarters, the county government, and the county anti-smoking association of this county held an anti-drug propaganda meeting at the Zhongnan Grand Theater at 9 AM on the 26th. About 2,000 people, including representatives of various institutions and organizations, military police, and students, attended. The presidium members, including Longti Yao, Li Tiping, and Qian Sunqing, successively reported on the progress of anti-drug efforts and advocated for the complete eradication of drugs in the Republic of China year 26, with all drug offenders being sentenced to death. Leng Yuqiu, a member of the Provincial Anti-Smoking Association, also came to Wuxi to participate and delivered a speech. At 1 PM in the afternoon, Leng, accompanied by Hua Jinji and others, went to the county drug rehabilitation center, the smoker's prison, and various opium dens in the urban area to inspect the situation in detail. In the rural areas, an expanded anti-drug propaganda meeting is scheduled to be held on the 28th in Shiqi Town, the Ninth District, to awaken all smokers as soon as possible and help them escape from suffering.

Two Homicide Cases Occurred

Yu Guiquan and Qian Bingfang, residents of Yanjiaqiao Township in the Seventh District of this county, had a conflict with A Er, a resident of Liqi Township, over collecting two "Jiao" of mat money, resulting in A Er's death from suffocation. The murderer has been transferred to the court for interrogation and detention. Unexpectedly, Xu Asheng, a 45-year-old farmer from Wujiali near Hongshengli in the Eighth District, whose original wife Shao had passed away, remarried a woman named Wang as his stepmother on February 25 of this year, and she is now six months pregnant. The eldest son has married a daughter-in-law, and the two daughters have also grown up. Asheng and his neighbor Wu Ada worked together to farm. On the evening of the 25th of this month, Xu and Wu were using a boat to transport rice to the threshing floor. Asheng complained that Ada was tying the rice too loosely, which led to an argument. Then, Ada struck Asheng on the head with a carrying pole, causing blood to flow like a waterfall, and he collapsed in the field, gasping for breath. Seeing that he had caused trouble, Ada hurriedly asked someone to carry Asheng back home and bandaged the wound for him. However, due to excessive blood loss, he died at around 2 AM. Xu's family immediately rushed to report to the Seventh Branch of the Public Security Bureau, and the Branch Chief Li Junjian led the police to arrest the murderer. After a preliminary interrogation, he was transferred to the county bureau. On the morning of the 26th, Wang Jinbao, the head of the 72nd district, reported the incident to the District Court. In the afternoon, the prosecutor led officials to the township for an inspection and re-examination.

Changzhou: The County Government Trains Monks and Taoists

The Wujin County Government recently received an order to organize training for monks and Taoists. On the 25th, it summoned the abbots of various temples and Taoist abbeys for a discussion. As a result, it was decided to start the training in early next month. The quota for the first phase of training is 180 people, including 120 from Tianning and Qingliang temples, and 60 from Chongfa, Longxing, Chongsheng, Xianqing, Fangsheng, and Xuanmiao Taoist abbeys. The training period is set for one month, on a half-day basis. Classes are held in one place, and the trainees return to their respective temples and abbeys for accommodation. The instructors have also been hired separately.

After the Yuehan Railway's Zhuping section was taken over by the Zhegan Railway, there were no major changes in personnel. Jiangyin: Fire Amidst Severe Drought

Since the beginning of autumn, there has been no rain for two months, and the weather has been severely dry. At 1 PM on the 25th, a fire suddenly broke out in the home of Qian Huaibai at No. 1 Buzhengfang in the city. Qian works in the National Government Military Affairs Office, and there were only women at home. When the fire broke out, it was difficult to put it out because there was no water in the city river. The fire destroyed several houses.

Gaoyou: A Big Fire Kills Two People

In the home of farmer Wu Jiuming, a household in Jiaba, Sibei Township, Sixth District of this county, a fire broke out accidentally at about 9 PM last night, causing a conflagration. In an instant, the fire illuminated the sky, and with the wind blowing strongly, the fire took advantage of the wind and spread like wildfire. The fire did not extinguish until about 12 midnight. All the more than ten houses and all the clothing, utensils, and deeds were reduced to ashes. Wu's 60-year-old father and 9-year-old daughter were both sound asleep and unable to escape. The two died in the fire. In addition, a Mauser rifle was also destroyed. The total losses are estimated to be about 6,000 yuan.

Luhe: Notorious Local Opium Dealer Arrested

Liu Hongsheng, a notorious private opium dealer in Zhudun Town, the Sixth District of Luhe County, has committed crimes repeatedly but has never been brought to justice. Wang Zhisan, a special investigator appointed by the Department of Civil Affairs, disguised himself and went to the town on the 20th. The county government ordered two bailiffs, Zhao Junfeng, to assist. When they arrived at Liu's residence, Liu realized that things were not good and resisted with a Mauser pistol. Fortunately, the gun misfired, preventing a disaster. The investigators disregarded their own safety and guarded Liu's door to prevent him from leaving. Liu's wife and many followers then rose up and beat the investigators violently. While they were holding each other, Li Hengkun, a town guard from the town, led many people and rushed in through the back door, letting Liu go. At that time, Li was arrested and taken into custody by the bailiffs. The bailiffs rushed to the district office to report and ask for assistance, but the district office had no armed assistance. They then telegraphed the county government to send a team. County Magistrate Qi was furious after learning the situation and immediately sent the security team leader Yan Shusheng to lead the team to assist in the arrest. Liu Hongsheng was arrested and sent to the county for legal punishment.

Zhucheng Yuegou Town: Unexpected Disaster Strikes, Villagers Perform a Play to Celebrate a Bumper Harvest, A Bomb Suddenly Falls from the Sky, More Than Sixty People Are Injured and Killed

Qingdao Correspondence: A person from Zhucheng said that Shangkou Village, Yuegou Town, in the northeastern part of Zhucheng, is now peaceful after the completion of agricultural work. It has specially raised funds to perform a play and share the peace and prosperity. Unexpectedly, at about 10 PM on the 19th of this month, while the gongs and drums were beating and thousands of people were moving, a bomb suddenly flew from the sky and fell into the crowd, causing a deafening explosion like thunder. Nine people were killed on the spot, including five from Shangkou Village, one from Xiangyue Village, one from Zhangjia Village, and two from Wutai Village. Eight people were seriously injured, and about fifty people were slightly injured. After the incident, the play was immediately stopped, and Zheng Ziqing, the dean of Liangjiazhuang Minsheng Hospital, was invited to treat the injured. The origin of the bomb was also investigated, but the matter was quite miraculous. Although the local militia thoroughly investigated, nothing was found. The village head has reported to the county government and is handling all the aftermath.

Domestic Goods Manufacturers Respond to the "One Day" Movement, This Is the Minimum Expression of Patriotism, The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Has Officially Collected Donations

The Municipal National Goods Year Games yesterday sent letters to the National Goods Maintenance Association, the Municipal Citizens' National Goods Consumption Association, the Machinery Industry Association, the National Product Manufacturers Association, the National Goods Factory Association, the Production and Sales Cooperative Association, the Industrial Federation, and other national goods organizations, requesting them to uniformly promote the "One Day" Movement initiated by the "Li Bao" newspaper to enrich national salvation preparations. Now, domestic goods manufacturers, having received the Chamber of Commerce's notice earlier, have responded and supported the movement. Some have sent their donations to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for collection. The details are recorded as follows:

Letter from the National Goods Association:

To the esteemed recipients: This year, we are pleased to celebrate Chairman Chiang's fiftieth birthday, and the completion of national unification is also worth celebrating. Various places are enthusiastically purchasing airplanes to celebrate his birthday. The "Li Bao" newspaper has initiated the "Contributing One Day to the Country" movement. The purpose of this movement is for factories and shops to contribute a portion of their monthly business income, and for employees to contribute all of their daily salary income to the government for the purchase of airplanes to celebrate the birthday and enrich national defense. We believe that the establishment of a country in the world depends on national defense. With the recent advances in science and technology, and the daily renewal of weapons, all countries are striving to build their air forces. Our country is currently in a time of increasing foreign aggression and national crisis. It is imperative to save resources and contribute to the country in order to resist aggression and save the nation. Chairman Chiang has made outstanding contributions to the party and the country. Dedicating an airplane to Chairman Chiang is dedicating an airplane to the party and the country. Therefore, this association expresses deep sympathy for the "One Day" movement initiated by the "Li Bao" newspaper and believes that this is the minimum expression of patriotism by the Chinese people and a touchstone of our patriotic hearts. We believe that your esteemed association, which is enthusiastic about patriotic movements, will have the same feeling about this. Therefore, we request you to lead your members to carry it out uniformly. The nation and the people will rely on it for true benefit.
