Fancy goods such as velvet, straight tribute, and serge have also gradually fallen (per yard) by 5 li to 1 fen. Printed velvet continues to fall (per yard) by 1 fen due to the cheap sale of hand goods. In view of the continuous decline in prices, various customer gangs have unanimously reduced purchases and are eagerly trying to unload their inventory, so new transactions are increasingly bleak. The factory's delivery of white goods, fancy goods, and grey cloth is still very tense.

Grains: Wheat Prices Do Not Loosen, Flour Market Still Rises

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the prices for each month showed an initial flat and continued rise. Because the quotations for foreign wheat had a difference of one or two jiao, the sentiment was still flat when the opening price was quoted. The opening price for the current month was only 3 yuan, 7 jiao, and 3 and a half fen. November and December also appeared flat, but to January and below, because off-site sentiment saw that the reserves were not abundant and the grain prices in various locations continued to rise, the buying was very strong, so the opening price was good by one or two fen. Then, bulls in the industry returned to sell, and it was slightly weaker again. Until the afternoon opening, because the end-of-month settlement was approaching again, the shorts gradually entered, and the market sentiment turned firm. In the distant months, because the factory's hedging was quiet again and the spot wheat market has not yet loosened, the sentiment continued to be stable. People in the industry speculate that if the distribution in the north stops, the wheat market will inevitably be dragged down, and the flour market will gradually ease.

Grain Prices in the North Step Up, Wheat Market Feels Increasingly Bullish

Yesterday's futures wheat market, after the opening in the morning, although the foreign wheat had a rise and fall of one or two jiao, the grain prices in the north gradually soared. Furthermore, the recent weather is still clear and smooth, and the sentiment inside and outside the industry can't help but feel anxious. Therefore, the transactions in each month were stable and appeared to be good, which was better than the previous week's closing price by one or two fen. Until the opening in the afternoon, the sentiment in the near term was still stable due to the settlement relationship, but to January and below, because there were few customer hedges and the wheat reserves were increasingly empty, the sentiment felt even stronger, so the uplift was even more intense. According to this situation, the sentiment cannot be expected to fall unless it approaches foreign wheat. The spot wheat market is still stable. High wheat such as Shaheji and Yaowan wheat is still quoted at 6 yuan, and Hankou fine wheat is as high as 5 yuan and 7 jiao, deciding to 5 yuan and 3 jiao. The total market is estimated to be 18,000 to 19,000 bales.

Oil Market: White Tung Oil Spot Goods Are Extremely Popular

It has been ten days since the new white tung oil was seen from the Zhejiang route. However, the arrival of goods was extremely slow due to the shallow water of the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, resulting in the interruption of spot oil in Hangzhou. The price was still 49 yuan per dan a few days ago. Then, due to insufficient supply, it immediately increased to 50 yuan. Recently, it has increased again to 52 yuan, all of which are paid in Shanghai and can only be handled in one or twenty dan, and it is still necessary to have arrivals assigned as a number. Most of the new futures sold by various producing areas in the past cannot be delivered on time, resulting in the fact that oil companies in this city have no spot goods to sell, and the shortage of reserves is extremely rare. Foreign firms in the Hankou market also pay attention to futures oil and only handle spot oil as needed. Therefore, occasional transactions are in the minority. The prices are between 51 and 2 yuan, foreign regulations. Futures oil has been handled until January, and the price is between 48 and 9 yuan, with a total of 3,000 to 4,000 tons traded, and the amount handled by various foreign firms in various producing areas in Sichuan and Hunan provinces is not included.

Narrow Strip Iron Spot Goods About to Run Out of Stock

Since narrow strip iron has been purchased by cigarette factories, canning factories, etc., the market has become very active. However, new goods have not arrived, and existing stocks are extremely scarce, so that spot goods in the market are almost completely sold out. The market price for ordinary colors is 26 yuan per case, while the price for individual sales ranges from 22 to 29 yuan (due to different sizes). Yesterday, various can factories and toy factories were also buying, and the future trend seems to continue to be optimistic.

Securities: In a Tug-of-War, Bond Market Shows Slight Fluctuations

Yesterday was the last day for October futures trading at the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange. Market conditions were entirely passive, influenced by the back-and-forth between short and long positions. Although there wasn't a major storm of activity, there were still traces to be found. Category C stocks remained consistently bullish, reportedly driven by a single entity in the financial sector holding a large long position. Category A stocks were heavily shorted, with prices being driven up significantly each day. Given these uncertain circumstances, it's difficult to predict any real improvement in the market. Today, only November futures will be traded for one month, which could bring about more changes. Yesterday's session opened with a chaotic market, with ups and downs depending on the relationship between long and short hedging. For example, Category D stocks were squeezed higher by 3.5%, while Category B stocks were squeezed up by a smaller 2%. Each category behaved differently. In the secondary market, there was some buying interest, but long hedging continued. The difference between near and far-term contracts for Category D stocks was excessive, leading to some long hedging and arbitrage, showing a near-term decline and a far-term rise. Other categories were slightly better, ranging from 0.1 to 0.4%. After the afternoon opening, there was a general upward trend. Category A stocks were heavily shorted and rose another 0.4%, while the other categories remained balanced. At the close, the market returned to a chaotic state, with highs and lows intermingling, with only about 0.1% upward movement. The final market results showed that only Categories E and C stocks fell slightly by 0.1%, while all others rose, with Category A rising the most at 0.6%. The total trading volume was 10,035,000 yuan. The following is a comparative table of the results of the price changes: (Unit: Yuan, Trading Unit: 100 Yuan)

Finance: Gold Market Extremely Quiet, Short Positions Slightly Covered Mid-Session, Swap Rises to 2.7 Yuan

The gold market started weak but strengthened later, with little activity in the middle, making it extremely quiet. Short positions were covered somewhat, resulting in a stable rise of 0.7%. In the morning, the overseas silver market saw London flat and the US market paused. The forward silver price in Montreux also remained unchanged. Exchange rates opened flat and closed slightly higher. The London spot gold price was unchanged. The Central Bank's posted rates were flat for both the British pound and the US dollar, and the customs gold unit was unchanged. The standard gold price remained at 1156.4 yuan. Pre-market trading opened lower at 56.5 yuan, but trading volume was light. When Wan Xing entered the market to buy, the price was immediately driven up, rising to over 7 yuan. The morning opening was high, and speculative short sellers took advantage of the situation. Major players also supplied some gold, but the market lacked support and immediately fell. Spot dealers bought in slightly at the lower prices, causing a rebound. The Hong Kong and Shanghai Banking Corporation's posted rates and the silver equalization tax were unchanged. The market then became extremely quiet, lacking movement and fluctuating only slightly until noon. The trend remained peaceful. The later market trend was initially weak but then stabilized, with major short players covering their positions. Sellers were scarce, and the market struggled to find counterparties, leading to a gradual rise. The Indian silver price initially rose one anna, then retreated slightly one anna a second time, but the final trend remained firm. Swaps suddenly rose to 3.7 yuan yesterday. The day's market is recorded as follows:

The morning opening was 1157.3 yuan, 0.5 yuan higher than last Saturday. Small investors such as Ding Kang, Yuan Mao Yong, etc. sold slightly, causing the price to fall to 6.4 yuan. Sheng Yuan Yong took advantage of the lower price to take delivery, raising the price to 7 yuan. The Hong Kong and Shanghai Banking Corporation's posted rates were flat for both the British pound and the US dollar. Yuan Mao Yong, Ding Kang, Heng Yu, etc. continued to supply gold. The silver equalization tax was also unchanged. Later, the price fell again to 6.6 yuan. Fu Xing Yong, Zhong Kang, etc. bought in slightly. The noon closing was 1156.9 yuan.

The afternoon market opened at 1156.8 yuan. Qia Feng Yong and Yuan Mao Yong sold off, causing the price to retreat to 6.6 yuan. Chun Yuan and Yong took advantage of the lower price to buy in, gradually driving the price back up. Cheng Da entered the market with a limited order to buy, further strengthening the price. The closing price rose to 1157.5 yuan.

The settlement price, based on the Central Bank's standard gold price, remained at 1156.4 yuan, about one yuan higher than the closing price. Registration prices were 1153 yuan for this month, 1155 yuan for November, and 1157 yuan for December. Morning interest was 1153 yuan. Red gold was priced at 6 yuan above, at 1163.3 yuan. The spot market was stable, with red gold priced at 13 yuan above. Tong Feng and Heng Sheng Yuan Yong each sold over 100 taels. The buying price was 8 yuan above. Tianjin goods were priced at 11.25 yuan above, but there were no transactions. The swap was yesterday offered to Da De Cheng by Heng Yu for 35 units at 1.7 yuan. Da De Cheng offered to Cheng Da 7 units at 1.6 yuan. Chun Yuan Yong Jing Fu offered to Da Da 200 units at 2.7 yuan.

Market trading was not particularly active. In summary, Fu Xing Yong, Shen Kang Cheng Da (offered 109 units to Zhu Yuan Yong at 57 yuan), Da De Cheng, Tong Feng, Heng Chun Yuan Yong, Niu Yuan Yong, etc. were on the buying side, while Heng Yu Yuan Mao Yong Xiang, Bian Da Feng Heng, etc. were on the selling side. Yuan Mao Yong and Ding Kang sold first and then bought. Wan Xing and Niu Yuan Yong bought first and then sold.

The day's market started weak but then stabilized. The opening price was 1157.3 yuan, and the closing price was 1157.5 yuan. The highest price was 1157.5 yuan, and the lowest price was 1156.4 yuan, with a fluctuation of 1.1 yuan. The result was a continued increase of 0.7 yuan compared to last Saturday. There were 224 remaining units of this month's notes, excluding government bonds, and 2359 remaining units of December notes. There were a total of 5 long positions and 14 short positions. There were 6202 units of December futures, with a total of 37 long positions and 30 short positions. The total trading volume was 875 units in the morning session and 434 units in the afternoon session.

Yesterday, the short position Da Feng Heng paid off 56 units to the exchange. The long positions that should receive today are: Da Chang Xiang Fu Tai Heng Qia Feng Yong 14 units each, Da De Cheng and Ding Kang 7 units each. The settlement price was 1153 yuan.

Exchange Market Even Less Change

The exchange market was stable yesterday, with no changes in overseas markets. The morning began with overseas cables reporting that London's long and short terms were flat. The New York silver market was closed, and the forward silver price in Montreux remained unchanged across the board. The British pound against the US dollar was unchanged, the US dollar against the British pound rose 0.09375, and the US dollar against the French franc fell 1.5 pence. The London spot silver remained unchanged. The Central Bank's posted rates were flat for both the British pound and the US dollar. The customs gold unit was unchanged. Thus, the exchange market was even more stable. The morning opening for the near-term selling price was 1 shilling, 2 pence, 4375 half-pence, the US exchange rate was 19.5 yuan, the same as last Saturday, for both the British pound and the US dollar. The Hong Kong and Shanghai Banking Corporation's posted rates were flat for both the British pound and the US dollar, and the silver equalization tax was unchanged. Banks engaged in some counterparty transactions, and there were swap transactions, but Chinese merchants tended to observe. The process was difficult to change. Chinese merchants banks such as Shanghai rose while Guohua matched it. At noon, it remained sluggish. There were both buying and selling in the afternoon. The Japanese bank was suppressing it, but Dalian was still maintaining it. The Indian silver price initially rose one anna, then retreated slightly one anna a second time. The final result was still flat. The closing selling price for the near-term was 1 shilling, 2 pence and 6875, and the US exchange rate was 29.5 yuan, unchanged from the previous close for both the British pound and the US dollar. Banks mostly engaged in counterparty transactions, and Chinese merchants were still inactive. The day's transactions are recorded as follows:

The morning opening for the near-term selling price of the British pound was 1 shilling, 2 pence, 4375, and 1/2 halfpenny. Mai Jia Li sold 46875 to a foreign firm for October, Da Ying sold 40625 to Mai Jia Li for December, and Hong Kong and Shanghai sold 34375 to You Li for February. In the afternoon, Mai Jia Li sold 40625 to Dong Ya for December, and Hong Kong and Shanghai sold 34375 to Mai Jia Li for February. The closing price was 1 shilling, 2 pence, 4375, and 1/2 halfpenny for spot, the same price for October, 40625 and 4375 for November, 375 for December, and 3125 and 34375 for January. Buying prices were adjusted upward.

The opening spot price for the US dollar was 29.5 yuan. Da Ying sold 0.5 yuan to Mai Jia Li for October, Shanghai sold 25 to Dalian for January, Hua Qi and Shanghai sold 25 to Guohua for January, Dong Fang sold 4375 to Hua Qi for November, and San Jing bought 0.5 yuan for October. The noon closing selling price for the near-term was 29.5 yuan. In the afternoon, Shanghai suppressed 0.5 yuan for October, Hua Qi lifted 4375 for November. The closing selling price was 29.5 yuan for spot, the same price for October, 4275 and 375 for November, 3125 for December, and 1875 and 15 for January. Buying prices were adjusted upwards by 0625.

North-South Goods: Shantou Candied Tangerine Peels Rise Another Yuan or So

The arrival of Shantou bridge peels has been scarce recently. More than a dozen pieces were continuously replenished the other day, and it was heard yesterday that they have been released. Because dealers need them, the supply cannot meet the demand, and the market is very good. Therefore, the opening price has risen by another yuan or so compared to before. According to news from the dealers, only a dozen pieces have been processed in the later batch, and the market price is not easy to ease.

Sugar Market: Domestic Green Sugar Sales Slow

Yesterday, the sugar market trend was flat and soft. The guild's planned price was 21.65 yuan for second-grade granulated sugar for immediate delivery, and 6.2 yuan for re-exported goods. The spot price for Dongbai No. 4 was 21.68 yuan, and the re-export price was 6.4 yuan. The spot price for No. 8 was a little more than 0.05 yuan, at 21.35 yuan, and the re-export price was 6.25 yuan. The spot price for No. 9 was 11.1 yuan, and the re-export price was 6 yuan. The price for No. 1 fine white sugar from local factories such as Zhen Ji, Jin Xin, and Da Hua was 20.5 yuan, and the prices for Nos. 2, 3, 4, and 5 were discounted. Domestic Chaoqing and miscellaneous green sugars had slow sales, and the market was stagnant. After four rounds, the prices were not announced, and the trend was weak.

The joint company's sample exchange period was yesterday, the first time this week. The total quota for Guangdong sugar was 6765 bags. The bid price remained unchanged. 965 bags of coarse white sugar from the Shunde factory were sold at 21.5 yuan, 40 bags from the Shixin factory were sold at 21.3 yuan, and 20 bags from the Quxi factory were sold at 21.1 yuan. Another 100 bags were sold at 20.9 yuan, and 130 bags of medium granulated white sugar were sold at 19.4 yuan, for a total of 1255 bags.

Metals: Pig Lead Prices Continue to Rise

Although the trading volume of pig lead has not been high recently, the arrival of goods has been very small, and the inventory in Shanghai is low. Therefore, the holders of the goods have a very good mindset. The market quoted price yesterday was 0.5 yuan higher than before, selling at 26 yuan per dan. There were some transactions with the Sichuan gang and factories, with 200-300 strips reportedly being sold. Transactions on the organ side have been relatively deserted recently.

Couplets from Twenty Years Ago

— (Hu Junfu)

At the beginning of the Republic of China, people in Shanghai held a grand and enthusiastic memorial meeting for the revolutionary martyrs who supported the revolution in the Gengzi year (1900). The meeting place was set up in Zhang Garden. The ink from songs and tears was like clouds. I wrote many couplets, the longest of which were two. One of them said: Who doesn't read the Spring and Autumn Annals? We are ashamed of you for your great righteousness. How can we recognize robbers as fathers? The heroic souls transform into hundreds of millions. Every drop of blood, every drop of tear, future generations will come, but there are no predecessors. From the long hells, we wave our hands to observe the chaos. To make the people prosperous, the revolution traces back to literary statements, which is in accordance with Heaven and the people. According to the rules of the world, don't ask about the past, present, and future. The wind is bleak, the rain is bleak, the wise men have knowledge, and freedom is immortal. Follow my ancestor, the Yellow Emperor, riding the dragon to Kunlun. Another couplet said: We, our ancestors, were born to support us, to this day, 4609 years. Lay the foundation for prosperity and create happiness for the common people. Tracing back to the first achievement, it was good to subdue the dragon and tame the lion, risking red blood and black iron to compensate for the price of all kinds of undertakings. Why sigh at the kylin and phoenix? Use heroic figures as special names for someone. Although the words are like people, the vigor is unparalleled. They are written on white silk more than ten feet long. The writer was Mr. Li Jingzhi, a calligrapher from my hometown, who has also passed away for a long time. A shorter couplet said: The situation creates heroes, and heroes create the situation. A man is not afraid of death, but afraid of not being a man. Also, my late friend Weng Jun Peifu wrote: The clouds and thunder are gathering, and you are suffering from their difficulties. Heaven and earth are being opened up, and we are coming to see its completion. The writing is concise, and the words are like casting, dignified like the person. Also, a couplet by my late friend Yun Tieqiao said: The country has no pigeons, or still hesitates at both ends. Alas! How can there be a revolution without bloodshed? Who is afraid of death? I only give way to you, saying: This is a hero who creates the situation. The words are sharp and like a historical discussion. Soon after, Yuan Shikai, when he was in power, gradually plotted to become emperor. The restrictions were very strict, and the whole country was fearful. At that time, I was depressed and unhappy. I happened to see a orchid exhibition in the local park, so I wrote a couplet: What era is this? My feelings are trustworthy. The upper and lower couplets only have eight characters, which is the shortest. Alas—the traitorous treaty that the whole country was unwilling to recognize, Yuan Shikai also planted the seeds of disaster at this time.

Skipping Rope Examination

— 19

The game of skipping rope is quite loved by children. Especially when the weather is cold, whether in the home, at school, on small streets, or beside thoroughfares, you can often see those children in groups of three or five; counting one, two, three, four in their mouths, their legs jumping up and down, playing this game. Moreover, playing this game is simpler than kicking shuttlecock. Kicking shuttlecock still requires people to prepare a shuttlecock. Those who lack this tool often cause disputes and arguments due to envy and jealousy: only playing this skipping rope, as long as you find a rope at random, everyone can have fun for a while.

Skipping rope belongs to jumping exercise. It not only can make the foot muscles developed, but also can make the blood circulate throughout the body. At the same time, it can also cultivate children's neat habits and the concept of counting. Therefore, this game, like kicking shuttlecock, is beneficial to the body, and wise parents and elementary school teachers do not prohibit it.

Skipping rope and kicking shuttlecock are both children's games in the north, and their origins are also very ancient. Liu Tong of the Ming Dynasty quoted a common saying "willow tree dies, kick shuttlecock" in his "Dijing Wulue". Dijing is now Beijing. This is talking about kicking shuttlecock. As for skipping rope, it was already very popular in the Northern Qi Dynasty. "Book of Northern Qi, Post Lord Ji": "Children playing games like to hold a rope with both hands and sweep the ground and jump on their feet, and sing 'Gao Mo'." According to the "Book of Northern Qi", the founding of the Northern Qi Dynasty was in 1362 years before the Republic of China, and it ended in 1335. Based on this, the game of skipping rope has a history of nearly 1400 years. According to the "Book of Northern Qi", the way of playing skipping rope was the same as today; and singing "Gao Mo" while jumping is enough to show that children's psychology is competitive, and the past and the present are the same. Also, jumping and singing are enough to match the rhythm, and the lively feeling is also visible.

The origin of skipping rope that can be investigated is like this.

Paper Cutting

— Qiao Yun Su

Paper cutting is one of the professions of women, and they can also be regarded as street artists. Three-inch golden lilies, wearing embroidered shoes, six-inch round skin, also wearing embroidered shoes. The author recently interviewed two "paper cutting" women, one middle-aged woman and one young girl who is waiting to be married. The young girl was a little shy and I didn't chat with her. The middle-aged woman gave me some information: every woman loves to wear embroidered shoes, but without the pattern, she can't embroider them by hand. A tall building that stands in the clouds, no matter how magnificent it is, doesn't it first require the architect's design? A pair of bright and dripping embroidered shoes, a paper cutting pattern, is equivalent to the architect's design; women in inland cities love to wear embroidered shoes. In fact, although European styles are blowing in the cities, they still can't avoid a pair of embroidered shoes on their wedding night; there are many women's shoe rooms in Shanghai's small gardens, aren't they displaying pairs of dazzling and brilliant embroidered shoes? The women who cut paper patterns, I don't know who the ancestor was? But they have been passed down from generation to generation, and they don't teach this kind of cutting skill to outsiders. They register with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, and it is a permanent patent; their sailboat is their home, and they regard the four seas as their home. Most of them are from Xinghua and Taixian in Jiangsu. Changzhou, Wuxi, Benniu, and Danyang in Jiangnan are their colonies; men repair umbrellas and kerosene lamps, and women cut paper patterns. They are not afraid of floods or droughts, and they don't suffer from unemployment. Everyone relies on their hands to buy food, enjoying the happiness of husband and wife singing in harmony; they often travel around, seeing and hearing a lot. They have an umbrella and a bag. We hear the sharp "paper cutting!" This kind of shouting is their way of attracting customers, like "peddlers"; an umbrella can resist the sun and rain, and a bag is like a "complete collection of books", which is also a miniature of the pattern room. Editor, scissors and paste, they use scissors and white paper. Although they have rough hands and dark skin, if you give them a pattern, they will cut it out accurately. When they encounter a girl who is about to get married, they are their only big customer; "rabbit watching the moon", "intertwined mandarin ducks", "lotus and lotus seeds", "butterflies flying through flowers" are all their masterpieces; when their business is good, they can earn five or six cents a day. Most of them are in groups of two, and when they meet a third or fourth colleague, they divide the income equally; they know that sailing in the same boat and mutual assistance are sacred rules.

Swapped Mandarin Ducks

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 7: High Brotherly Affection, Hiding Letters and Pitying Weak Sister, Strong Poetic and Scholarly Air, Peeping Shadows and Laughing at Poor Scholars

Youmei said: "Because in this summer, when there are no orchids, you still display things with the same name as orchids. When there are real orchids, how can you not like them?" Guoqi smiled slightly and nodded twice, only saying "Please sit, please sit." Youmei sat down on the rattan chair by the table. She turned her head casually and saw a piece of artificial rock in a porcelain pot, which was very exquisite and translucent. The green moss on it was half an inch long, and the small tree seedlings and fluffy fine grass were matched with small figures, which was quite interesting. Just as she was paying attention to it, she saw another square cattail pot next to the rock pot, with a letter pressed under the pot. The envelope was a thick, white, foreign-style one. There was a raised rose on the opposite side of the envelope's opening. Because the letter was facing upwards, there were no words on it. But Youmei had seen this kind of envelope in Menglan's study. According to her, this kind of envelope is not available in Beijing now; they are brought from Shanghai. Could it be such a coincidence that they were all brought from Shanghai? She thought like this, but she immediately became alert. How could she look at other people's secrets when visiting their house? So she picked up the plaster goddess and looked at it, laughing: "This house is very elegant, but adding such a statue is too fashionable and doesn't match these furnishings." Guoqi sat down on the rattan chair in the distance and laughed: "Many friends say the same thing when they see this thing. I explain it to everyone. This is an ancient Western myth. This female statue is the goddess of love, but unfortunately, she is oppressed by the god of misfortune and lost her freedom. Her name is Venus. Because her fate is very bitter, I find it has some poetic flavor, so I often put her on the table to help my writing." Youmei said: "So that's how it is. Why doesn't Cousin put the statue of the goddess of freedom on the table?" Guoqi laughed: "Do you think that present-day China can talk about any freedom?" When Youmei heard this, she put down the plaster statue and looked at Guoqi's face. She felt that his face had a layer of melancholy at that moment. (90)

New Bouncy Ball Talk

— Huang Nanding

Ever since bouncy ball opera came to Shanghai, every amusement park has been decorated with bouncy ball opera, and it has reached its peak. In these few years, many bouncy ball opera troupes have come to Shanghai. As for those currently performing in Shanghai, there are: Xicailian at the Daxin Amusement Park, Furonghua at the Xinxin Garden, Zhangcailan at the Sincere Amusement Park, Zhu Baoxia at the Great World, Bai Yushuang at the Empire Theater, as well as Yu Lingzhi, Xiang Lingzhi, Ai Lianjun, Xiao Bai Yushuang, etc. However, Zhu Baoxia holds the record for bouncy ball opera in Shanghai, and Zhu Baoxia is currently the most popular. Since Zhu Baoxia came to Shanghai and performed at the New World Hotel, Shanghai people have begun to pay attention to bouncy ball opera. Recently, the bouncy ball opera with the best business at each amusement park is the Great World, which is almost always full. Therefore, the most popular and commendable bouncy ball opera in Shanghai is Zhu Baoxia's troupe, especially Baoxia and her sister Zixia.

No matter what kind of drama, if it only sticks to the original scripts and does not rehearse new dramas, it will never have lasting appeal. Especially bouncy ball opera, the original scripts are all crude and simple. Although there are a few better scripts, such as "Peach Blossom Temple," "Du Shiniang," and "Li Xianglian Selling Paintings," without creating new bouncy ball operas, it will not arouse the audience's interest. However, creating new dramas is not an easy task, and it requires experience in writing dramas, good teachers, and good materials. Bouncy ball opera has not been paid attention to for a long time, so it is naturally very difficult to find such talents. Now, Zhu Baoxia has obtained the guidance of the famous Peking Opera teacher Guan Hongbin, so the new dramas she performs cannot be compared to ordinary bouncy ball operas.

Among Zhu Baoxia's new dramas, the best one is "The Fox Spirit Fate." Zhu had also performed new dramas before, such as "Blood and Tears Tablet," "Sai Jinhua," and "Yu Tangchun," but none of them had as interesting and wonderful plots and tight scenes as "The Fox Spirit Fate." Because "The Fox Spirit Fate" script is very suitable for the conditions of drama. There are large sections of singing, delicate expressions, and all the supporting roles can fulfill their duties, especially Zhu Zixia, who has both sadness and happiness, which can make Baoxia have the effect of red flowers and green leaves. Moreover, Baoxia has a large section of erhuang singing in the script, and the tune is very similar to Chen Yanqiu, and her voice is loud and cloud-piercing, and can split metal and stone, making the whole drama more colorful. Therefore, since the premiere of the new drama "The Fox Spirit Fate," it has been widely praised, and Zhu Baoxia's artistic success has been further consolidated.

Miscellaneous Talk

Shanghai's Insects

— Tai Shang

Shanghai, this place is truly marvelous and unbelievably contradictory. You could say it has everything, or you could say it has nothing!

Shanghai is a place that only consumes and doesn't produce. Such a large city can't even find a single authentic local product. Besides those spoiled sons of rich families, seductive women, and cunning merchants? Even everyday necessities like firewood, rice, oil, salt, fish, shrimp, and vegetables have to be imported from elsewhere. However, all the world's wealth is gathered in Shanghai, so the specialties of all places also converge here. As the saying goes, "Money can make the gods move." As long as you have money, unless it's a dragon's liver, a phoenix's marrow, or a mosquito's bone, things that don't exist in the human world, Shanghai has every other strange and precious item you could want. Even all kinds of rare birds and fierce beasts, and creatures from icy mountains and snowy seas, like tigers, leopards, rhinoceroses, elephants, bears, orangutans, kangaroos, seals, sturgeons, etc., which are rare and hard to find in China, some people will go to great lengths to transport them from afar to display them in zoos and amusement parks. There are also performers from circuses like the "Haijing Bo Circus," who come from tens of thousands of miles away, sailing across the ocean to perform for us. This is all because "this master has plenty of money!"

However, the power of money sometimes has its limits. There are many extremely tiny and ordinary things that are rare and hard to find in Shanghai. Guess what these precious things are? Haha, they are the insignificant "insects"!

Originally, "wood rots, then insects are born." Insects mostly grow in damp and filthy places, hiding in forests and weeds. But Shanghai is full of nouveau riche, where "buildings are tall, trees are small, and everything is un-ancient." There are also regulations that require buildings to be rebuilt within a certain number of years, not allowing any dilapidated old buildings to exist. Furthermore, most of the residents live in "jewel box" style alleyway houses, where you can't see a single leaf when you look up, and you can't find a single blade of grass when you look down. So, where can insects find a place to breed and multiply? Moreover, the sanitation authorities have repeatedly emphasized cleanliness, equipped with new and sharp tools, and rigorously sweep away everything, making them even more "without remnant," and "unable to rest." As a result, things become valuable when they are rare. Like the crickets in Chancellor Jia's half-room, or Mr. Jia Huan's frogs in the Grand View Garden, or the cicadas silently standing in the corridors of temples, their remaining sounds dragging the country down with each branch. In Shanghai, they are actually as precious as white pigs from Liaodong, peddled from afar to "await a good price!"

The mainland has many pests, especially mosquitoes in the summer, which are as noisy as thunder and suck blood, acting like public enemies of humanity. West Lake can be called a summer resort, but it also suffers from having many large mosquitoes. Although it's not as bad as the "Laughing Forest Records" say, "Arriving at Yanziji in the morning, the mosquitoes are as big as chickens; staying overnight in the Wushan Gorge, the mosquitoes are bigger than ducks," (?) it's not much different from "Lu Jin Shrine." Therefore, places like Liu Zhuang, the lakeside houses are all equipped with special mosquito nets made of green gauze. Shanghai originally doesn't have many mosquitoes. The prosperous areas of the concession have no grasslands or "stagnant water" nearby, so you can spend the whole summer without needing a mosquito net, which is something that the mainland can never do.

I have lived in Shanghai for nearly twenty years, and I think this is the only advantage of Shanghai, but when watching outdoor movies at the Dahua Hotel (?), this statement should be retracted!

Shenbao Medical Journal

A Study of Germ Warfare (Part 2)

— Li Lingdong

—A Special Report on the Eve of the World War

"Plague" is a general term for the practical result of germ warfare. It includes various infectious diseases. Each infectious disease is a molecule of the plague. The molecules are connected to form a plague. Therefore, the Chinese people cannot understand infectious diseases. When they encounter an infectious disease, they always use the term "plague." But a certain infectious disease has certain symptoms and signs (omitted here, please refer to special books). Regarding treatment, it is not very important in germ warfare. It is the same as ordinary treatment. The special point is that eradicating bacteria is the only guideline. The most important thing is to start with prevention, which is the most valuable thing. There are two principles that can be followed for methods of germ warfare defense that can be effective: (1) The responsibility borne by the state. Because the enemy uses germ warfare to attack us, all people in the country are harmed. It is not something that a certain province or a certain place can defend successfully. There must be defensive equipment and construction projects in the entire car so that it will not be threatened by the enemy and can strengthen its armed forces to defend the integrity of the country. (2) Training the people of the whole country to have a considerable understanding of germ warfare, organize epidemic prevention teams with epidemic prevention common sense to engage in epidemic prevention, so as to assist the country and strengthen prevention work.

In terms of personal defense practices, cultivate "daily life," "work and rest," dietary "cleanliness," and hygienic matters. How to maintain bone hygiene, how to maintain muscle hygiene? How to maintain the hygiene of the digestive, circulatory, respiratory, excretory, and sensory human body systems, so that the people of the whole country can obtain methods of personal hygiene and achieve a state of physical health. With a healthy national physique and an invigorated national spirit, they can resist diseases and bacterial attacks.

To ensure the safety of the property of the people of the whole country, human happiness, and avoid the harm of germ warfare, group prevention is the only effective method. It has been said above, and now it is listed below:

(1) Port Quarantine and Transportation Hygiene Management: Cholera is also called "Tiger Cholera." China did not have this disease, but it was spread from India. The spread from place A to place B is entirely through transportation as a medium. Now, science is prosperous and transportation is developed, so there are more opportunities for spread. Therefore, transportation hygiene management and port quarantine are very important in preventing the plague. At customs entry and exit points, travelers are checked. If anyone is found to have a suspected disease or carrier, they must not move freely and must be quarantined. This can prevent the plague in place A from spreading to place B. This type of impediment work is an indispensable facility.

(2) Immune Testing and Preventive Injections: There are many diseases that can be avoided by engaging in prevention early, such as cholera, typhoid fever, diphtheria, tetanus, rabies, scarlet fever, meningitis...etc. Early preventive injections have a tendency to reduce the occurrence of disease and lower the mortality rate. But we still have many other diseases. Do we have resistance? We do not know. Therefore, we must carry out immune tests on a large scale so that we can know whether someone can develop resistance to a certain disease, or lacks resistance and is easily infected. Then, inject antibodies to increase their immunity, so that the people of the whole country can resist the transmission of viruses.

(3) Eradication of Rats, Flies, Mosquitoes, Bedbugs, etc.: The source of many plague diseases is entirely due to a certain parasite as a medium. For example, bedbugs are the medium for typhus and relapsing fever. Flies are the medium for cholera, typhoid fever, and dysentery. Mosquitoes are the medium for malaria and yellow fever. Rat fleas are an important medium for plague. Therefore, the whole country should unite to eradicate these parasites.

(4) Management of Feces and Ditches: Feces and ditches are the locations of dirty things and are the source of infectious diseases and the birthplace of plagues. China has always not paid attention to the facilities and management of feces and ditches, so the high mortality rate is not unrelated to this. Therefore, the improvement of toilets, the disposal of feces, and the construction of sewers can no longer be delayed, as they are related to the survival of the country!

There are also several other inspection tasks that must be carried out and are related to people's daily lives, listed below:

(1) Water Inspection: The most important thing for hygiene is drinking water. The relationship between water and people is the closest. If you don't pay attention to hygiene, infectious diseases are easily caused. Therefore, water must be inspected at any time. The taste, color, ingredients, etc. of water must be strictly inspected before it can be used. If it cannot be used, it should be banned immediately. If examined under a microscope, if there are more than 150 bacteria in one gram of water, it should never be drunk.

(2) Food Inspection: Humans rely on the power of food every day to nourish their physique, replenish their physical strength, and regulate their body temperature. Diet is indispensable in the living environment. Since food is so important, it must be inspected to see if it is corrupt, if germs are parasitic on it, what is the nutritional price, and what is the degree of digestion? It has a serious relationship with human life.

(3) Air Testing: Air and life are inseparable by even a fraction. If breathing cannot provide a sufficient amount in an instant, a person can die immediately from suffocation. Therefore, we must check whether the air is fresh, whether it contains toxins, and whether germs are parasitic. This is something that we cannot ignore.

Regarding the disinfection after the plague is transmitted, a brief description is given below:

(1) Patients - Patients with infectious diseases must take a full body bath and change clothes when cured. If it is impossible, wipe clean with a warm, damp cloth to replace the bath.

(2) Corpses - Corpses with infectious diseases are best cremated. If not, when putting them in a coffin, sprinkle or soak the bedding with mercury bichloride or carbolic acid, and then fill it with lime.

(3) Transporting Patients and Corpses - The ropes, poles, and bedding used to transport patients or corpses with infectious diseases must be wiped with mercury bichloride or carbolic acid each time.

(4) Toilets and Ditches - Vomit and excrement from infectious diseases must be disinfected. If dung is used for irrigation and fertilizer, it must be disinfected for one week before it can be used as fertilizer. The soil in the ditches should be irrigated with lime milk for disinfection.

(5) Households and Houses - The interior of the households and houses of those who have infectious diseases should be wiped clean with carbolic acid or mercury bichloride, and then sunlight should be allowed to enter to dry it.

(6) Clothes and Utensils - The clothes and bedding used by those who have infectious diseases should be washed clean with green soap or wiped clean with carbolic acid.

(7) Cars and Ships - Usually sprinkle with carbolic acid, and then disinfect the vomit and excrement of those who have infectious diseases.

From the above, we can see that gas warfare is not to be feared, but germ warfare is an inhumane type of war. But in today's world, conscience is gone and justice is not obvious, so we can no longer ignore the study of germ warfare. The defense and construction of germ warfare should be the most important national policy in the rescue strategy to prevent emergencies. But we must not be overly afraid and trembling. In short, germ warfare is not easy to practice. Germ warfare will one day be practiced. Our only understanding is to prepare quickly! "Strengthening military power to protect the integrity of the country and seeking peace for the people of the world" is our current urgent plan!

Soviet Medical Circle's Research on Higher Nervous Activity

— Sound of Waves from Moscow

The research work of the Higher Nervous Activity Group of the All-Soviet Union Institute of Experimental Medicine includes all issues of nervous activity. From the early stages of embryonic tissue to the form of conditioned reflexes, the methods by which animals adapt to the external environment are all comprehensively covered. The basic question of its research work is the nervous activity organization related to the influence of surrounding activities. In short, this question involves central and peripheral nervous activity. Therefore, the research group has four laboratories: an Embryo Genetics Laboratory, an Experimental Neurology Laboratory, a Conditioned Reflex Laboratory, and a Morphology Laboratory.

The basic question of the first part of the research group's work is the extent to which the nerve center formed in the early stage of embryonic life is affected by the surrounding organs. This question is of particular significance because previous studies on nerve centers have believed that all components related to the nervous system before production are organizations that are rarely changed, especially for various parts of the central nervous system.

The experiment is carried out according to the following procedure:

In the early stage of embryonic development, the abdominal wall and uterus of the pregnant animal are cut open, and a brain incision is performed on the embryo to separate the various parts of the brain. After that, the uterus and abdominal wall are sutured and the pregnant animal continues its pregnancy life. After the operation, it takes about thirty to forty days for the embryo to reach its production. The first activity of this type of embryo in the external environment at the time of production is a very noteworthy thing.

If the operation is performed in the earliest stage, in most cases, the general activity of the newborn animal, its ability to develop conditioned reflexes, that is, its ability to adapt to the external environment, is very normal.

If the operation is performed in the later stage of life in the uterus, in most cases, the newborn animal has obvious defects at the time of production and it is difficult to adapt to its environment. For example, some animals lose the ability to move forward and can only retreat. Other animals can only stand in one place and jump up and down. Still others can only continue to rotate in one direction.

This type of newborn animal often loses the instinct to find its mother, but at the same time, it does not show any defects in other aspects. This type of newborn animal can stay by its mother's side for several hours without noticing or trying to breastfeed. The loss of this complex instinct is a definite sign of a change in the animal's general functional ability, but with long-term good care, it is still possible to return to normal completely.

Another noteworthy thing is that even if the operation is performed early and the performance of the newborn animal is very normal, abnormal distribution is often seen in the brain lobes when examined under a microscope.

The Higher Nervous Activity Research Group of the Soviet Union Institute of Experimental Medicine has performed this type of operation fifty times, most of which are studies of the situation after production.

The Role of Peripheral Organs

Regarding the role of peripheral organs, the conclusion of the experiment is as follows: The central nervous system is affected by the impulse of peripheral organs very early. Therefore, during this period, the tissue changes of the central nervous system, even if the organs have not yet formed their own nervous system, can be compensated by the slow impulse of the peripheral organs. In short, the impulse of the peripheral organs to the nerve center can make the already changed central nervous system form a normal functional relationship. This is the historical role of peripheral organs as the main builders of nervous tissue.

Therefore, this experiment again supports the basic point of view of the nervous activity research group.

The second part of the research group's work is about the experimental changes in the nerve center.

The main method of this work is to connect the peripheral organs with the nerve center, but not to make the peripheral organs belong to the nerve center. The completion of this type of work is due to the connection of nerve trunks, such as the vagus nerve, which is a nerve for the throat, heart, and intestines, to connect a nerve for the limbs. Then its normal relationship with the central nervous system is hindered. Thus, any stimulation of the front leg, each contraction of the muscle, is transmitted to another part of the central nervous system. The result of this connection can cause confusion in the central nervous system. For example, a dog has a coughing reaction to scratching its leg. The sudden sound when the muscles stretch can promote a lasting, stubborn vomiting performance. These phenomena can arouse the special interest of scientists. Long-term observation of these phenomena and their evolution can help us understand the permanence of certain nerve centers.

Research on Nerve Centers

In addition, the animal's reaction often depends on the condition of the nerve center. For example, the animal's leg begins to breathe with breathing

Page 16

Breathing, or with swallowing, shows all the complex actions of eating, etc. In this way, we can study the characteristics of each nerve center.

The research group further studied to try various different stimuli, especially paying attention to stimuli with profound physiological significance, and transferring the stimulation of the eye to the same nerve center as above. Therefore, the vagus nerve was sutured with the optic nerve and the sensory nerve of the eye. As a result, within four months, any slight contact of the cornea of the eye with a piece of paper provoked a strong cough, and eventually vomiting. Thus, we can see that the skin and cornea are stimulated, as if the stimulation directly reaches the vagus nerve center.

There is also a more sensitive surface for receiving stimuli, namely the mucous membrane.

For experiments transmitted from the mucous membrane, the surface of the tongue is often chosen. Therefore, the vagus nerve is sutured with all the tongue nerves in order to transfer the stimulation received by the tongue to the vagus nerve center, instead of reaching its original nerve center. As a result, coughing and vomiting were again provoked, which was the same as the phenomena of the above experiments.

There are many similar experiments, all different.

This kind of observation over several years is very important. From the experiment, we see the fixation of some nerve centers and the easy variability of other nerve centers. In some cases, the peripheral impulse is attached to the nerve center to rebuild its work. In other cases, on the contrary, the nerve center often strongly controls the organ (muscle) to work according to its own will for a long time.

These experiments have been done on hundreds of animals, allowing us to conclude that the general assumption that nerve centers are immutable based on the immutable characteristics seen in some specific nerve centers is wrong.

The main feature of this experiment is the change of the nerve center, and sometimes it is possible to tell in advance what kind of change will occur in the functional center.

The third part of the research group's work is the research of advanced nervous activity. The research method used is very special. There are two research methods. One is Pavlov's conditioned reflex method. This method has made many important achievements for the establishment of the theory of brain activity. In addition, there is a method of studying whole body actions, such as the method of the American behaviorist school. The research method of the group is to combine the above two methods into a new method. When experimenting with dogs using the Ba method, letting the dogs move freely, in addition to secreting saliva after receiving conditioned stimuli, the dogs also look around as if trying to find the source of the stimulation. Therefore, the experimenter also pays attention to the actions of the experimental animals at the same time, which can not only study in detail according to Ba's conditioned reflex, but also carefully examine the dog's actions.

The result of using this research method is that we can get a wide range of research on animal nerves. According to the research of this method, there are more than 20 scientific reports, and its future development is unlimited.

More on the Problem of Blood Transfusion

— Song Guobin

Since I published "A Question of Blood Transfusion" in this journal, a few days later, a certain lawyer's reasons for requesting the Lawyers Association to transfer the explanation to the Ministry were published in this newspaper. I was originally unwilling to comment further, but because this matter is of great importance and is related to medicine, the medical profession, and social hearing, I hereby write this to challenge it.

The lawyer said: "According to Article 22 of the Criminal Law, legitimate acts in the course of business are not punished." The so-called legitimate acts, in terms of the medical profession, are the implementation of a legitimate operation on the patient himself when necessary... Blood transfusion is to save one person while harming another... It cannot be regarded as a legitimate act."

Difficult to say: "Whether blood transfusion is a legitimate act should depend on whether blood transfusion can cause harm. As for whether it can cause harm, it cannot be determined by empty words. There must be medical and clinical proof. Roughly speaking, the blood of ordinary strong people is as much as five or six liters, and each extraction is only a small amount of more than one hundred cubic centimeters. Extracting a hair from nine oxen will not damage the health of the blood donor. And in terms of clinical experience, the blood of the person being drawn is produced faster and supplemented more easily due to repeated extractions. Therefore, blood transfusion is actually a scientific therapy that uses the excess to make up for the deficiency, and there is no harm at all. Cutting off A's limbs to supplement B, or cutting off C's nose to give to D is indeed harmful behavior and cannot be compared with blood transfusion. However, since there is no harm, it is naturally a legitimate act and is undoubtedly among those that are not punished."

The lawyer said: "The criminal law recognizes the degree of crime based on the result when the implementation begins. As for whether it can be restored later, the law does not ask."

Difficult to say: The lawyer's words are in response to my previous article "The person being bled can recover after a little rest." The criminal law's so-called determination of the degree of crime based on the results at the time of implementation refers to those who knowingly start implementation knowing that the results are bad. As for the matter of blood transfusion, the doctor clearly knows that bleeding will not cause harm, and also knows that blood transfusion can have a curative effect. At the time of starting implementation, he already knew that it would be beneficial and harmless. How can it be called a crime? If the lawyer's words are to be believed, and blood transfusion is directly recognized as a criminal act, then the medical profession is bound by the law, and even the requests of benevolent fathers, filial sons, benevolent brothers, close relatives, religious people, and patriots can only be rejected and firmly refused. Why? Cannot agree to voluntary harm. This makes the filial watch the death of their relatives, the benevolent cherish the warm blood of sacrifice in vain, and traps the medical profession in enduring people. (End)

Common Sense Q&A About Diseases

— Cheng Hanzhang

(94) Chronic Articular Rheumatism

(Question) What is called Chronic Articular Rheumatism?

(Answer) It is like acute articular rheumatism (see 59), also a type of polyarthritis, but progresses very slowly.

(Question) How does this disease occur?

(Answer) Some are secondary to acute polyarthritis, some develop chronically and progress latently from the beginning, and some are caused by other diseases. Such as syphilitic chronic arthritis, gonorrheal chronic arthritis, or tuberculous chronic arthritis, etc.

(Question) Is there any relationship between this chronic articular rheumatism and gender?

(Answer) It is more likely to occur in women.

(Question) Does it occur in children?

(Answer) Rarely. However, symmetrical joint swelling in children, accompanied by swelling of the lymph glands and spleen, is a dangerous type of septicemia, specifically called Still's disease.

(Question) What are the symptoms of chronic articular rheumatism?

(Answer) The main symptom is affecting the small joints, with pain during movement or pressure: there is a feeling of stiffness in the joints upon waking up. If forced to move, there will be cracking or grating sounds. This pain and stiffness are related to the weather and will worsen during the rainy season.

(Question) Are there any abnormalities in the appearance of joints affected by chronic articular rheumatism?

(Answer) They mostly become deformed. The hand develops spindle-shaped swelling at the metacarpal and phalangeal joints. The second phalanx bends like a dislocation, turning towards the back of the hand and bending outwards. The first phalanx often assumes an overextended position. The bones and muscles become atrophied.

(Question) What condition does the skin of the affected area exhibit?

(Answer) The skin above the affected joint is smooth like it has been painted, with a glossy appearance, and sometimes pigmentation occurs.

(Question) How is it treated?

(Answer) For chronic articular rheumatism, the first step is to find the cause and treat the underlying disease. It is essential to pay attention to dry living conditions and eat easily digestible foods. As for treating the disease itself, it can be divided into drug therapy, local therapy, and hot spring therapy.

(Question) What is drug therapy like?

(Answer) First, use a small amount of salicylate preparations for several days to relieve pain. Atophan is also effective; also, take iodine preparations and arsenic preparations internally.

(Question) What is local therapy like?

(Answer) Apply camphor liniment or iodine tincture, or salicylate application, alcohol compress. Perform hot steam baths, electric hot baths, warm compresses, artificial sun lamp irradiation, diathermy, and congestion therapy on the joint area.

(Question) What about hot spring baths?

(Answer) Simple spring water, or carbonic acid springs, sulfur springs, etc., are all acceptable. If these are effective, then perform warm river baths, radioactive mineral springs and other therapies.

Hygiene Common Sense of Eye, Ear, Nose and Throat Diseases (104) Olfaction

— Tang Renjin

Our nasal cavity generally has three functions: breathing, olfaction, and assisting in the formation of speech. Therefore, if a disease occurs in the nasal cavity or the whole body, these three functions can be affected or obstructed sequentially. Now, let me briefly talk about olfaction.

The function of human olfactory organs is slightly weaker compared to the functions of other five senses. This is because it has fallen into a state of degeneration. Therefore, our sense of smell is not very sharp. Conversely, for example, mammals such as dogs, cats, and rats have particularly developed senses of smell. Therefore, dogs can explore their urine traces to know the route. Furthermore, police dogs can be trained to help police officers search for the tracks of thieves. These facts and successes are all due to the use of their keen sense of smell. Returning to the topic, the olfactory part of the human nasal mucosa exists in the mucosa of the superior and middle turbinates and the nasal septum mucosa opposite these two parts. A type of olfactory cell is distributed on this type of mucosa. If the odorant from the outside flows into the nasal cavity and invades the mucosa, then the odorant can stimulate the olfactory cells and cause odor perception. The strength of olfaction can be checked with the olfactory meter invented by Zwaardemaker to determine the size of olfactory power. Generally, in medicine, abnormalities in olfaction are collectively referred to as olfactory disorders. There are mainly four olfactory disorders: (1) hyperosmia, (2) hyposmia, (3) anosmia, and (4) dysosmia.

(1) Hyperosmia—is when the sense of smell is stronger than usual. It often occurs during hysteria, neurasthenia, menstruation, and pregnancy.

(2) Hyposmia—is when the sense of smell is weaker than usual.

(3) Anosmia—is when the sense of smell has become paralyzed. The causes of the above two types of olfactory disorders can be divided into central, respiratory, and true types. The central cause often occurs in brain diseases. The respiratory cause often occurs in nasal diseases, upper respiratory tract diseases, and lung diseases. The true cause often occurs in abnormalities of the olfactory nerve.

(4) Dysosmia—there are two types. One type is misidentifying the sense of smell containing a certain odorant as the sense of smell of another odorant. For example, smelling a fragrant odor and thinking it is a sour taste, or even thinking it is an unpleasant foul odor. This is called parosmia. One type is perceiving a certain odor even when there is no odorant present. This is called olfactory hallucination. These dysosmias are often seen in hysteria, neurasthenia, latent sinusitis, foreign bodies, and malignant tumors.

If you suffer from an olfactory disorder, you should immediately explore the underlying disease and treat it. Otherwise, it is often difficult to be effective.

On Rickettsia and Rickettsial Diseases (5)

— Chen Duanbai

When the rash initially appears, the systemic symptoms worsen accordingly, breathing also becomes difficult, the mind suddenly becomes blurred, the hands and feet twitch from time to time, and delirium occurs. The pulse rate increases dramatically, bowel movements become constipated, and urine becomes red and dark. If the condition takes a turn for the worse, then at the end of the second week, the patient, in a state of unconsciousness, may lose his life due to cardiac paralysis. The drop in temperature is usually rapid after two weeks. Urtsich suddenly drops from 40 degrees to normal body temperature within two or three days. It is also a common occurrence to have a sudden spike in temperature before or after the drop. At this time, the patient is tired and sleepy. After waking up, the mind is clear, as if waking up from a big dream. The recovery period is relatively short. Pneumonia is the most worrisome complication, and gangrene at the return site is also feared. The mortality rate of this disease can be said to be quite high, but it also varies with the epidemic season and climate. Usually, we set it at 20 percent. The prognosis for patients over 30 years old is more dangerous.

(8) Diagnosis

Pathological tissue examination reveals the special fact of blood vessel wall necrosis. Serum examination is the commonly performed Weil-Felix test, the Agglutination serum agglutination reaction of Prosenx × i9. Normally, i; 100 is considered positive, and there are also high values of i; 10000 and i; 20000. This reaction is almost always accurate after the sixth day, without any errors. However, its principle has not yet been satisfactorily explained. The differentiation between typhus and enteric typhoid fever is, of course, without doubt when the symptoms are clear. The spots can solve this problem. As for other systemic symptoms, patients with enteric typhoid fever exhibit a gloomy and quiet attitude, while typhus exhibits the opposite, with an unpeaceful mind. Clinicians can tell at a glance. The most precise distinction is, of course, the serum reaction. This is a non-speaking friend who will not deceive.

(9) Treatment and Prevention

The treatment of typhus and other Rickettsial diseases, because no absolutely effective drug has yet been found, serum treatment is also in the experimental stage, so everything is only symptomatic treatment, such as strengthening the heart, calming the nerves, detoxifying, promoting bowel movements, as well as ventilation of the room, and dietary care. Early use of metal preparations seems to have some beneficial effects. In general, the treatment strategy focuses on the protection of the circulatory system and the avoidance of complications.

The method of prevention, the application of immunological methods, cannot be discussed now. What can be done is the cleanliness of the residence and the extermination of lice. This disease is related to insects, so most of the people who suffer from this disease belong to friends who do not pay attention to hygiene in their residences or are unable to afford it, poor survivalists. Therefore, the active areas of Rickettsia in Europe are the small countries of Eastern Europe, Poland and Russia. Although there are fewer countries that pay attention to life, they have also learned a lot of lessons in the fierce battles in Europe. What about us! What should our country do? Should we first know where it is epidemic and where it exists?

Investigation Report on the Health Status of Xiaoshi, Zhejiang (6)

— Shen Songnian

(E) Conclusion

Although this article only pertains to the health conditions in Xiaoshi, if we expand our view to various parts of the country, we will know that some of its content can serve as a representative of Chinese health, because the health conditions in various parts of the country are mostly so bleak. From this, we further realize the immaturity of Chinese health. No wonder foreigners ridicule us as the "sick man of East Asia." So, how should we strive to catch up? Then the prosperity of the country can be expected, and the rejuvenation of the nation is hopeful! Otherwise, in the near future, I am afraid that there will be no color of our great China on the world map.

Now, the impressions and improvement suggestions after observation are further described below:

(A) Promote Health Education:

(1) Each school should add at least two hours of health education per week, and hire experts to give lectures to cultivate children's hygiene habits.

(2) Cultural institutions should form popular health lecture teams and tour around to instill health knowledge to the public at any time, with the principle of promoting public health.

(3) Schools should hire formal doctors as school doctors, and factories and families should also hire formal doctors with excellent experience as medical consultants.

(4) The medical community should also exert its natural duty at any time, do its best to instill health knowledge to the public, and strive to promote its popularization.

(5) The authorities should at any time order health police to force the public to attend lectures on health knowledge at designated locations by the stipulated date, and understand them within a time limit. Oral tests should be held at the end of the period. If life is still not in line with hygiene and does not pay attention to hygiene, immediate punishment will not be forgiven, in order to warn others.

(6) Screen health education movies, free of charge, to achieve the practical effect of popularizing health education.

(7) The social education section originally established by the education authority should be changed to the health education section, and experts should be hired to promote it, with the principle of achieving the popularization of health education and the development of health education in various schools.

(B) Improve Municipal Administration and People's Health

(1) Strange clothing, bare legs and arms, exposed chests, and applying rouge and powder are not only harmful to hygiene, but also harmful to public morals, so they should be banned.

(2) The health matters of restaurants and other places should be closely monitored by the authorities, and special regulations should be formulated for management.

(3) The authorities should order the old-fashioned old houses to open more windows to ensure that lighting, ventilation, and warmth can meet the minimum requirements of hygiene principles.

(4) Streets that have been in disrepair for many years are not only rugged and uneven, which is inconvenient for pedestrians, but even inevitably dangerous. Therefore, methods should be found to correct them.

More trash cans should be set up in streets and alleys, and the authorities should add more cleaners to implement cleaning work, and should engage in health publicity to make the public pay attention to public morality in order to promote and transform environmental sanitation.

(5) Establish public bathhouses for the common people, and everything must be for the common people and meet hygiene standards, and provide low-priced supplies to the public to cultivate good habits of bathing and protect the health of the people.

(6) Form a disease insurance savings association and promote a savings system in order to prepare for a rainy day, because disease is impermanent, and medical expenses are unavoidable. The moneyed class is certainly not worried, but most of the people are proletarians and their monthly income is very small and their income is limited. It is difficult to cope with illness, and even temporarily die because of insufficient financial resources. This is lamentable. Therefore, savings should be made in peacetime for use in times of illness.

(7) Establish more public medical institutions (such as district hospitals) to seek health protection for the common people and to seek welfare for the society. All medical expenses should be completely exempted in order to seek the universality of scientific medicine. This organization will also be responsible for free vaccination and preventive injections. The expenses will be generously donated by philanthropists.
